drang srong ri byi bsnyen zhing phyogs su ma song ba
yang dag skyed par byed pa'i lha mo mkhyen par mdzod BCt_9.26

ngang pa rnam par bral ba'i ngang mo lta bu dang
nags na glang po dang bral glang mo lta bu ni
mgon dang bcas kyang mgon med dman zhing nyam thag pa'i
btsun mo gzigs pa yis ni skyong par 'os pa yin BCt_9.27

sras gcig byis pa sdug bsngal 'os pa ma yin pa
kun nas gdung ba mthar gyur pa ni 'dren pa ste
gang ba'i zla ba sgra gcan nye bar bsgyur las bzhin
sgra gcan 'dzin de gnyen gyi mya ngan las thar mdzod BCt_9.28

pho brang btsun mo'i 'khor dang grong khyer mtha' dag ni
khyed dang bral ba'i bud shing can gyi mya ngan me
phyir 'byung dbugs ni du ba mun pa'i rtse mo yis
tshig pa dag ni khyed la lta ba'i chu 'dod do BCt_9.29

mdun na 'don pa de yi tshig dag gsan gyur nas
byang chub sems dpa' yongs su gang ba'i sems dpa' des
yon tan ldan zhing yon tan shes pas yud tsam zhig
bsam gtan mdzad nas rigs pa'i lan 'di smras pa'o BCt_9.30

pha rnams kyi ni bu la dgongs pa shes pa ste
gang zhig bdag la sa skyong gi ni khyad par du
shes pa yin yang na dang rga dang rgud pa las
'jigs te nags su phyin nas rang gi skye bo dor BCt_9.31

mthar ni gal te dga' ba dang bral ma yin na
rang gi skye bo dga' ba lta 'dod cis ma yin
gang tshe yun ring gyur kyang rnam par 'bral ba ste
de phyir bla ma brtse ba yin yang 'dor bar bgyi BCt_9.32

gang yang bdag gi ched du mi yi bdag po yi
mya ngan khyod kyis smras des bdag la dga' ba med
gang phyir rmi lam yang dag 'dus par 'gyur rnams su
rnam par bral bar 'gyur la kun nas gdung bar byed BCt_9.33

'gro ba'i spyod pa rnam pa sna tshogs mthong nas ni
de bzhin du yang khyod kyi blo gros nges par song
bu min gnyen min kun nas gdung ba'i rgyu yin bzhin
'ching ba de ni shes pa med pa'i mtshan ma nyid BCt_9.34

lam du 'gro rnams 'dir ni 'dus pa ja lta ba'i
skye dgu rnams ni dus su nges par 'bral ba ste
gnyen 'dun dam 'cha' skye bos rnam par dman pa yi
shes rab ldan pa'i skye bos mya ngan bsnyen nam ci BCt_9.35

gzhan du rang gi skye bo dor nas 'dir 'ongs la
'dir yang rab tu bslus nas slar yang 'gro ba ste
der song nas kyang pha rol gzhan du 'gro 'gyur la
de ltar 'dor ldan skye la rjes su brten rnam ci BCt_9.36

gang tshe mngal nas gzung ste gnas skabs thams cad du
gsod pa'i phyir ni 'chi ba rab tu gnas pa ste
bu la dga' ba der ni khyed kyis smras pa yi
bdag gi nags su brten pa gang phyir dus ma yin BCt_9.37

yul la mngon par lhung tshe dus ma yin pa ste
de bzhin nor gyi cho gar zhugs pa dus yin no
dus rnams kun tu dus kyi 'gro ba khyab pa ste
dge legs nges par thob la dus yod ma yin no BCt_9.38

gang yang rgyal pos bdag la rgyal srid 'dir bzhed pa
de yang yab kyi rgya chen mtshungs shing 'dra ba ste
sred pa las ni nad pa'i mi 'phrod zas bzhin du
bdag gi rab tu 'dzin par nus pa ma yin no BCt_9.39

gti mug rmongs pa'i gzhi ma mi skyong rgyal po nyid
rab tu 'thob par mi ni mkhas pas gang phyir nus
gang du skyo ba dang bcas rgyags dang ngal dub dang
pha rol log par spyod pas chos la gnod pa'o BCt_9.40

dza-mbu chu gser bzhin du gsal ba'i lding khang ni
dug dang 'dres pa'i kha zas bzang po lta bu dang
gza' yis 'khrugs pa'i padma dang bcas chu lta bu
rgyal srid dang ni gser dag sdug bsngal dag gi rten BCt_9.41

de ltar rgyal srid chos min bde ba ma yin pa
ji ltar mi gtsang skyes te mi dbang snga ma rnams
sdug bsngal yongs su spang bya na tshod rab mchog tshe
rgyal srid nges par dor nas nags su song bar gyur BCt_9.42

rin chen bzhin du tshim pa mchog ni nyer khyud nas
'brog dgon nag na rtswa dang zos pa mchog yin la
sbrul nag bzhin du mthong ba ma yin nyes pa ni
rnyed bla'i dpal dang lhan cig nyal ba mchog ma yin BCt_9.43

rgyal srid rnam par spangs pa rgyal po rnams kyi chos
mngon par 'dod pas nags su rab 'jug bsngags pa ste
nags tshal yongs su dor nas khyim du rab 'jug pa
dam bca' nye bar bcom pa'i 'thad pa ma yin no BCt_9.44

rigs su skyes shing sems pa dang bcas mi gang gis
chos ni mngon par 'dod pas nags su rab zhugs la
ngur smrig rab tu 'dor nas ngo tsha rnam spangs pa
grong khyer 'joms pa yi yang grong la bsnyen ma yin BCt_9.45

sred dang rnam par rmongs dang yang na 'jigs pa yis
gang zhig bskyugs pa'i bza' ba slar yang len byed la
sred dang de ni rmongs dang yang na 'jigs pa yis
'dod pa rnams ni dor nas slar yang len par byed BCt_9.46

gang zhig rab 'bar khang pa dag nas ci zhig ltar
byung nas slar yang de nyid kho nar rab 'jug la
nyes pa mthong de khyim na gnas pa dor nas ni
rmongs pas slar yang len par mngon par 'dod pa'o BCt_9.47

gang yang mi skyong khyim na gnas pas thar pa ni
'thob pa dang ldan zhes thos de ni med pa ste
zhi ba gtso bo'i thar pa'i chos ni gang la 'ang
chad pa gtso bo'i rgyal po'i chos ni gang du'o BCt_9.48

zhi la dga' ba gal te rgyal srid dman pa ste
rgyal srid la blo gal te zhi ba rnam par nyams
grang dang dro dang me dang chu yi gcig nyid bzhin
zhi ba dang ni rno nyid 'thad pa ma yin no BCt_9.49

me dang chu yi 'du ba yod pa ma yin la
khram dang drang po'i 'du ba yod pa ma yin zhing
'phags dang sdig pa'i 'du ba yod pa ma yin te
zhi dang chad pa'i 'du ba yod pa ma yin no BCt_9.50

de phyir sa 'dzin bdag po de rnams nges pas sam
rgyal po'i srid rnams spangs te zhi ba thob pa can
rgyal srid dag la snyen nas dbang po spas nyid las
mthar ma thug par thar bar mngon pa'i nga rgyal byas BCt_9.51

de dag rnams kyi rgyal srid la zhi ji lta bzhin
bdag ni nags tshal rab thob nges pas ma yin zhing
khim dang gnen gyi 'du shes zhags pa bcad nas ni
thar gyur slar yang rab tu 'jug par 'dod ma yin BCt_9.52

de ltar bdag nyid rnam shes yon tan rjes mthun pa
de 'dod spangs shing gtan tshigs ldan pa sgrogs pa ste
mi dbang bdag nyid skyes kyi smra ldan thos gyur nas
gsang sngags 'dzin pa yis kyang lan ni smras pa'o BCt_9.53

gang zhig chos kyi cho gas nges pa khyod kyi 'di
rigs pa min pa ma yin 'di ni dus rigs yin
na tshod la gnas yab ni mya ngan phyir byin nas
chos 'dod khyod kyi chos ma yin par gyur pa'o BCt_9.54

nges par khyed kyi blo ni shin tu phra min zhing
yang na chos dang don dang 'dod par mkhas ma yin
gang zhig ma mthong 'bras bu'i don du khyed nyid kyis
mngon sum don ni yongs su brnyas par mdzad nas gshegs BCt_9.55

yang srid yod ces kha cig dag ni smra ba ste
med ces kha cig dang ni nges par dam 'cha'o
de ltar gang tshe don 'di the tshom gyur pa ste
de phyir longs spyod par nus dpal ni nye bar gnas BCt_9.56

gal te slar yang rab tu 'jug pa gang yang yod
der ni ji ltar 'thad pa dag la dga' bar bgyi
ci ste gzhan du rab tu 'jug pa gang yang med
'gro ba 'di yi 'bad rtsol med las thar pa grub BCt_9.57

kha cig 'jig rten pha rol yod ces smra ba ste
thar pa'i sbyor ba la ni bsngags pa byed ma yin
ji ltar me yi dro dang chu yi gsher ba nyid
de ltar rab tu 'jug par rang bzhin nyid du smra BCt_9.58

dge dang mi dge nyid dang srid dang srid min la
kha cig rang bzhin las shes bsngag pa byed pa ste
gang phyir 'di dag thams cad rang bzhin las yin te
de yi phyir yang rab tu 'bad pa don med 'gyur BCt_9.59

gang zhig dbang po rnams kyi nges par rab spyod pa
yul rnams la ni dga' ba dang ni mi dga' nyid
gang zhig rga dang nad rnams dag gis sbyor byed de
de la gang gis 'bad dam de ni rang bzhin no BCt_9.60

chu rnams kyis ni me rnams zhi bar nye 'gro zhing
'od zer rnams kyis chu ni skems par byed pa ste
lus la yang dag gnas pa'i 'byung ba tha dad rnams
gcig nyid gyur nas 'gro ba dag ni 'dren par byed BCt_9.61

gang zhig lag pa rkang pa lto rgyab mgo rnams kyis
mngal du song ba'i ngo bo nges par sgrub byed la
gang tshe bdag nyid de yi de yis sbyor ba ste
rang bzhin las byung de shes rnams kyis de smra'o BCt_9.62

bya dang ri dags rnams kyi sna tshogs ngo bo dang
tsher ma'i rnon po nyid du rab tu byed pa su
rab tu 'jug pa 'di kun rang bzhin las yin la
'dod pa byed pa yod min 'bad pa gang las so BCt_9.63

de bzhin gzhan rnams dbang phyug las skyes smra ba ste
der ni skyes bu'i rab tu 'jug pa la don ci
'gro ba'i rab tu 'jug la gang nyid rgyu yin zhing
ldog pa la ni nges par de nyid rgyu yin no BCt_9.64

kha cig bdag gi mtshan ma nyid du smra ba ste
rab tu skye ba nyid dang srid pa zad pa yang
'bad pa med las rab tu skye bar smra ba ste
'bad pa yis ni thar pa 'thob par smra ba'o BCt_9.65

lha yi mchod sbyin drang srong rnams kyi rig byed dang
pha yi bu lon med pa bu rnams kyis te mi
gang gi grol ba yod pa de yi thar pa zhes
bu lon gsum po de dang lhan cig skyes pa'o BCt_9.66

de ltar cho ga'i bya ba'i rim pa 'di yis ni
'bad rtsol bcas pa'i thar pa de shes rnams smra la
'bad rtsol ldan pa yin yang rnam par gnon pa yis
thar ba 'dod pa rnams ni ngal ba thob par byed BCt_9.67

de phyir zhi ba gal te thar la gus yod na
cho gar brjod pa ji ltar rigs pas bsnyen mdzod dang
'di yi nye bar 'thad pa de ltar 'gyur ba ste
mi yi bdag po'i kun nas gdung ba nyams par 'gyur BCt_9.68

dka' thub nags tshal dag nas khang par 'jug pa la
khyod kyi skyon gyi blo gros gang zhig rab zhugs te
yab gcig der yang khyod kyi bsam bar ma gyur dang
snga ma rnams kyang nags nas rang gi khang par gshegs BCt_9.69

dka' thub nags na gnas pa bu rnams kyis bskor te
rgyal po a mba rī ṣa grong du zhugs gyur la
de bzhin 'phags min rnams kyis sa ni rnam bcom pa
dka' thub nags nas 'ongs nas rangs byed kyis bsrungs so BCt_9.70

de bzhin do ba dang bcas bdag po'i ljon shing ming
nags gnas bu dang bcas pa grong du zhugs pa ste
tshangs pa'i drang srong gyur dang thub pa gnas 'jog las
sbyin sreg dang bcas mtha' can lha yis dpal bzung ngo BCt_9.71

rnam pa de ltar chos dang grags par rab zhugs pa
nags rnams bor nas khang khyim rnams su song ba ste
de phyir dka' thub nags nas chos kyi ched du nyid
khyim na rab tu 'gro ba skyon yod ma yin no BCt_9.72

de nas mi skyong rgyal po'i dga' dang phan pa nyid
byas pa'i blon po de yi tshig dag gsan nas ni
dman min ma 'khrug chags min brtan dang gnas pa la
myur min tshig ni rgyal po sras kyis smras pa'o BCt_9.73

'dir ni yod dang med ces the tshom gang de ni
gzhan gyi tshig gis bdag la 'di na nges pa med
dka' thub dang ni zhi bas de nyid rtogs gyur nas
gang 'dir nges par bdag nyid kyis ni bzung bar bgyi BCt_9.74

phan tshun gnod cing mi gsal the tshom skye ba yi
lta ba dag ni len par bdag gi nus ma yin
mun par long bas long ba'i lam mkhan byed pa bzhin
mkhas pa'i skye bo su zhig gzhan gyi rkyen gyis 'gro BCt_9.75

de nyid ma mthong gyur kyang 'on kyang kho bo yi
dge dang mi dger the tshom na dge blo gros gyur
'bras bu med bying la yang dge ba'i bdag nyid mchog
smad pa'i bdag nyid de nyid la yang bde ba med BCt_9.76

rnam bzhag med pa'i lung 'di yang na mthong gyur nas
tshad ldan rnams kyis gang smras de ni legs rtogs mdzod
nyes la rab dman tshad ldan nyid ni rtogs mdzod dang
nyes pa rab tu dman gyis bden min smra ba min BCt_9.77

khyim la 'jug par dmigs gang bdag la khyod kyis ni
smras shing rangs byed la sogs rnams ni dper bstan te
de rnams tshad min chos nges rnams su nus med cing
tshad ma'i ched du brtul zhugs rnams ni yongs su zad BCt_9.78

de lta na yang nyi ma sa la lhung gyur la
gangs dang ldan pa'i ri bos brtan nyid 'dor na yang
de nyid ma mthong yul la kha bltas dbang po ni
khyim rnams dag la so so skye bo mi bsnyen to BCt_9.79

bdag ni 'bar bar gyur pa'i me la 'jug pa ste
don ma byas par khyim gyi gzhi la rab mi 'jug
de ltar thugs rgyal ldan des dam bca' mdzad gyur cing
ji ltar 'dod bzhin bzhengs nas ngar 'dzin med par gshegs BCt_9.80

de nas mchi ma dang bcas blon dang gnyis skyes gnyis
de yi brtan pa nyid dang nges pa thos gyur nas
yi mug bzhin ldan rjes su song nas sdug bsngal ba
dal bus song nas grong khyer nyid du song bar gyur BCt_9.81

de nas de la brtse dang mi skyong la gus las
de dag ltos bcas rab tu song zhing gnas gyur la
gsal zhing snang bas nyi ma blta bar dka' ba ltar
de ni lam du blta bar ma nus dor bar min BCt_9.82

mchog tu gshegs de gshegs pa shes phyir de dag gis
so pa'i skyes bu gtsang ma sbas pa rnams byas nas
dga' zhing sras po 'dod pa'i rgyal po la song nas
ji ltar blta 'am zhes ni ji ltar yang song ngo BCt_9.83

| sangs rgyas kyi spyod pa zhes bya ba'i snyan dngags chen po las | gzhon nu rjes su tshol ba'i le'u ste dgu pa'o ||

sku sto rgyas shing rgya chen rgyal po'i sras po de
bsreg bya dang sngags bdag po de dag rnams spangs te
dba' rlabs g.yo ba'i chu bo ganggā brgal nas ni
dpal dang ldan pa'i rgyal po'i khab tu gshegs par gyur BCt_10.1

ri rnams dag gis legs par sbas dang brgyan pa dang
dge dang dka' thub gter bas gzung dang gtsang ba ste
zhi bar rab byung tshangs pa mtho ris logs su bzhin
ri lnga mtshan ma'i grong khyer rab tu thob par gyur BCt_10.2

zab mor gyur pa'i mdangs ngar de yi lus gsal ba
skyes bu rnams ni shin tu gnon pa mthong gyur nas
khyu mchog rgyal mtshan de yi brtul zhugs brtan pa bzhin
der ni de tshe skye bo rnams ni ya mtshan gyur BCt_10.3

de rab mthong nas gzhan gang ma song de gnas shing
der ni gang zhig lam na gnas de rjes 'gro zhing
gang zhig skyen par song de brtan por song gyur la
kha cig bsdad pa gang yin de ni langs pa 'o BCt_10.4

skye bo kha cig de la mchod pa'i lag pa yis
bsti stang byas nas kha cig mgo bos phyag 'tshal zhing
kha cig mnyen pa'i tshig gis mngon par stod byed cing
kha cig de la rab tu mchod nas song bar gyur BCt_10.5

de rab mthong nas sna tshogs cha lugs rnams ngo tsha
rab bkram tshig ni lam du smra ba med par song
dngos su bzhin du chos rnams dag gi nye logs su
kha cig tshul ma yin pa'i blo gros ma gyur to BCt_10.6

lha dang mtshungs pa'i mi dbang sras po de mthong nas
bya ba gzhan ma rnams kyang rgyal po'i lam du ni
mchod mang bkir sti sngon 'gro bud med rnams kyi 'am
skyes pa rnams kyi mig dang ngom par ma gyur to BCt_10.7

dpral ba'am smin ma dag dang zhal lam spyan dag dang
sku 'am phyag dag dang ni 'gros sam zhabs dag ni
gang gis de yi gang nyid der ni mthong gyur pa
de nyid kyis ni de yi mig dag bcings par gyur BCt_10.8

smin ma mdzod spu dang bcas spyan dag yangs pa dang
sku lis mdzes shing dge ba'i dra ba dang ldan phyag
sa skyong nyid du 'os pa'i dge slong cha lugs de
mthong nas rgyal po'i khab kyi phun tshogs g.yos par gyur BCt_10.9

de nas khang pa'i phyi nas rnam rgyas skye bo'i tshogs
ma ga dha yi khyim gyi jo bo bzo spyangs kyis
mthong bar gyur te de yi rgyu mtshan dris pa ste
de nas 'di la skyes bu rnams kyis de smras so BCt_10.10

yi shes mchog gam yang na sa yi dpal dag ni
thob par 'gyur zhes bram ze rnams kyis gang smras pa
rab tu gshegs par skye bos nges par mthong ba yi
shākya'i bdag po'i sras po de ni 'di yin no BCt_10.11

de nas don thos yid kyis chags shing zhen gyur pa'i
rgyal po'i sa ni skyes bu de nyid la smras pa
de ni gang du song zhes rnam par shes par mdzod
de nas de ltar bgyi zhes skyes bu rjes su song BCt_10.12

g.yo min spyan ni gnya' shing gang tsam gzigs pa ste
gsung ni kun nas snyoms shing zab mo'i 'gros mnga' ba
g.yo ba'i sems dang lus rnams dag ni nges bsdams nas
dge slong mchog nyid de yang bsod snyoms la gshegs so BCt_10.13

ji ltar nye bar 'thad pa'i bsod snyoms bsnams nas ni
rnam par dben zhing char rab 'bab par rab gshegs la
der ni tshul bzhin rigs pas mngon par gsol gyur nas
de ni sa 'dzin ri bo skya bseng la 'jogs so BCt_10.14

ro dhra'i nags kyis nye bar sbas pa'i ri bo der
rma bya'i skad kyis rab gang lo ma'i spyil po na
'char ri'i steng na nyi ma gzhon nu ji lta bar
ngur smrig gos kyis nyi ma'i nyi ma de mdzes so BCt_10.15

der ni de nyid rgyal po'i 'khor de mthong gyur nas
bzo sbyangs rgyal po la ni gtam ngag byas pa ste
thos nas rgyal po des kyang mchod pa mang po las
der ni sbas pa'i rjes su 'brang bas rab tu song BCt_10.16

skya bsong ri bo mchog la skya bseng na dang ni
brtson 'grus mnyam zhing ri bo dang mnyam sku lus can
mi yi seng ge'i 'gros can cod man 'dzin pa ste
ral pa g.yo ba'i seng ge bzhin du 'jogs par gyur BCt_10.17

de nas de yi steng na rtse mor gyur pa yi
byang chub sems dpa' dbang po nye bar zhi ba ni
ri bong gi mtshan sprin gyi sbubs nas byung ba bzhin
skyil mo krung gis bzhugs nas rnam par mdzes pa mthong BCt_10.18

gzugs dang phun sum tshogs dang nye bar zhi ba yis
chos kyi sprul pa bzhin du nye bar bzhugs de la
ya mtshan dang bcas rab tu bsnyen ldan mi dbang po
rang byung la ni brgya byin gyis bzhin nye bar gnas BCt_10.19

rigs pa yis ni rigs pa rig pa rnams kyi mchog
khams mnyam gyur pa de la song nas dris pa ste
de nyid kyis kyang mtshungs shing zhi bas mi skyong la
yid ni rang bzhin gnas dang nad med smras par gyur BCt_10.20

de nas gtsang la glang po'i rna ba ltar sngo ba'i
rdo ba'i logs la rgyal po yang dag nges gnas shing
nye sar nye bar bsad nas rjes su mthun pa yis
de i dgongs pa rnam par shes 'dod 'di smras so BCt_10.21

rim pas 'ongs pa nyid dang yongs su brtags pa ste
khyod kyi rigs kyis bdag gi dga' ba mchog yin la
gang phyir bdag la rang gi na tshod smra 'dod pa
skyes te de phyir brtse ba'i tshig 'di mkhyen par mdzod BCt_10.22

khyod kyi rigs ni rnam rgyas sngon du nyi ma ste
lus kyang na tshod gsar pa gsal la mdzes pa 'di
gang phyir 'di ni khyod kyi blo gros rim med pas
slong mo nyid la mngon dga' rgyal srid la ma yin BCt_10.23

khyod kyi lus 'di tsan dan dmar po 'os pa ste
ngur smrig gis dkris de ni 'os pa ma yin no
lag pa 'di ni skye dgu skyong bar 'os pa ste
gzhan gyis byin pa'i bza' ba za bar 'os ma yin BCt_10.24

de phyir zhi ba gal te yab kyi rgyal srid la
khyod kyis yab kyi brtse las stobs kyis mi 'dod cing
khyod kyi blo gros rim par bzod par ma gyur na
skyen par kho bo'i yul gyi phyed la longs spyod mdzod BCt_10.25

de lta na ni rang gi skye la gnod min zhing
dus kyi rim pa yis kyang dpal gang bsngags pa ste
de phyir khyod kyis bdag la brtse ba mdzod cig dang
dam pa rnams dang bcas pas dam pa'i dpal 'phel lo BCt_10.26

ci ste da ni rigs kyi khengs pa nyid las ni
bdag cag rnams la khyod la blo gtad yon tan med
sde rgyas rnams ni mda' yis rnam par dkrugs byas nas
bdag dang bcas pas pha rol rnams ni pham par mdzod BCt_10.27

de phyir 'dir ni gnyis dbus gcig blo tshol mdzod la
chos don 'dod pa rnams la cho ga bzhin bsnyen mdzod
'di na sde tshan gsum po chags las rnam zlogs nas
'di dang gzhan du phyin nas lhung ba kun nas 'thob BCt_10.28

gang zhig don dang chos la gnod nas 'dod pa dang
chos dang 'dod pa yongs su brnyas nas don dang ni
'dod dang don dag nye bar zhi bas chos de ni
don byas gal te mtha' dag 'dod na don yin no BCt_10.29

de phyir sde tshan gsum la nges par snyen pa yis
khyod kyi gzugs 'di 'bras bu bcas pa nyid du mdzod
chos dang don dang 'dod pa dman min thob pa la
mi rnams dag gi dman min skye ba'i don du smra BCt_10.30

de phyir gzhu ni rnam par 'gengs 'os rgyas pa'i phyag
'di dag 'bras bu med par byed par 'os min te
nga la nu bzhin 'dis ni 'jig rten gsum rnams kyang
pham par 'os pa yin na sa 'dir smos ci dgos BCt_10.31

brtse bas nges par de ni bdag gis smra ba ste
ya mtshan gyis min dbang phyug nyid kyi chags pas min
khyod kyi dge slong nyid kyi cha lugs 'di mthong nas
rjes su brtse ba skyes nas mchi ma yang byung ngo BCt_10.32

de phyir rang rigs rab mtshungs khyod kyi gzugs ji srid
rga bas zil gyis mnan nas slar yang ma 'ongs par
slong mo'i gnas 'dod 'dod pa rnams la longs spyod la
dus su chos la dga' ba chos ni gyis mdzod cig BCt_10.33

'khogs pas nges par chos ni 'thob par nas pa ste
'dod pa nye bar spyod la rgyas pa'i 'gro ba med
de phyir dar la bab pa'i 'dod pa rnams smra ste
bar ma'i nor yin rgan po rnams kyi chos yin no BCt_10.34

gson pa'i 'jig rten dag na chos dang don dag ni
rnam par 'gal bar gyur pa yin phyir lang tsho rnams
yang dag bsrung ba yin yang thub par dka' ba ste
gang phyir 'dod pas lam de las ni 'phrog par byed BCt_10.35

na tshod 'khogs pa rnams ni rnam dpyod ldan pa ste
shin tu brtan pa'i gnas skabs mchog tu song ba rnams
ngo tsha ba nyid phyir dang song ba ma yin phyir
'bad pa nyung ngus zhi ba'i bdag nyid 'gyur ba 'o BCt_10.36

de nyid phyir na g.yo zhing yul ni gtso bo dang
rab mos bzod pa ma yin ring por mthong min la
'brog dgon dag las nges par thar nas dbugs phyung bzhin
g.yo sgyu mang po'i lang tsho shin tu 'das nas so BCt_10.37

de phyir mi brtan g.yo la bag med ldan pa yi
na tshod gsar pa 'di ni re zhig rnam par 'ong |g 54b
'dod pa'i lta yi sngon du na tshod 'ben yin la
dbang po rnams las bsrung bar nus pa ma yin no BCt_10.38

ci ste khyed kyi chos nyid mdzad par 'dod pa ni
mchod sbyon kyis lha mchod mdzod 'di ni rigs kyi chos
mchod sbyin rnams kyis mtho ris logs ni byin rlabs nas
lha dbang nyid kyang mtho ris logs su gshegs par gyur BCt_10.39

gser gyi dpung rgyan rnam par bcings pa'i phyag rnams dang
nor bu'i sgron mas 'bar ba'i dbu rgyan sna tshogs can
mi skyong drang srong rnams dang drang srong chen po rnams
ngal bas gang gshegs 'gros der mchod sbyin rnams kyis gshegs BCt_10.40

de ltar ma ga dha yi bdag pos tshig smras pa
gang zhig dbang po'i bzhin du smra ba yang dag mdzes
sna tshogs du ma'i sa phyogs ti se'i gangs ri ltar
rgyal po sras des de thos gyur nas nam ma g.yos BCt_10.41

sangs rgyas kyi spyod pa zhes bya ba'i snyan dngags chen po las | bzo sbyangs sngon du song ba'i le'u ste bcu pa'o | |

de nas bshes kyi sgo nas phan pa yin pa'i don
de ltar ma ga dha yi bdag po smras pa yis
rang gnas rnam par 'gyur min rigs gtsang gcang ba'i
zas gtsang rgyal po'i sras kyis tshig 'di smras pa 'o BCt_11.1

seng ges mtshan pa'i yangs pa'i rigs su rab skyes pa
khyed kyi cho ga de ni ngo mtshan che ma yin
gang phyir bshes gnyen phyogs su gshegs 'dod khyod kyi ni
yongs su dag pa'i spyod pas spyod pa de yin no BCt_11.2

rang rigs rjes su spyod pas dam pa min la byams
dbang po ma tshang ba la dpal bzhin gnas min la
snga mas byas pa'i dga' ba rim rnams kyis
de ni dam pa rnams kyis rnam par 'phel bar byed BCt_11.3

don ni dka' ba rnams su mi rnams gang zhig gis
mdza' bo rnams kyi nam pa'i don gyur 'jig rten na
bshes gnyen de rnams blo yis yongs su shes bgyi ste
rang gnas dag ni 'phel bar gang phyir ma yin BCt_11.4

de ltar gang gis rdzas dag thob nas 'jig rten na
bshes rnams dang ni chos la nges par sbyor byed pa
de rnams kyi ni nor gyis snying po thob pa ste
mthar ni nyams las gdung ba skyed par byed ma yin BCt_11.5

rgyal po mdza' bo nyid dang 'phags pa nyid kyis kyang
khyod kyi nges pa gang zhig bdag la dmigs pa 'di
mdza' bo nyid kyis 'dir ni rjes su bsnyad bygi ste
rgol ba gzhan min 'dir ni bdag gis smra bar bgyi BCt_11.6

bdag gis rga dang 'chi ba'i 'jigs pa rnam rig nas
thar pa 'dod pas chos 'di rab tu thob pa ste
gnyen 'dun dga' ba mchi ma'i gdong ldan rnam spangs nas
mi dge'i rgyur gyur 'dod pa rnams ni sngon nyid do BCt_11.7

bdag gi yul rnams dag las ji ltar 'jigs pa nyid
de ltar sprul gyi dug rnams la ni mi 'jigs shing
nam mkha' dag las 'phos pa'i thog rnams las min la
rlung dang bcas pa'i me rnams dag las ma yin no BCt_11.8

mi rtag 'dod pa rnams kyis dge ba'i nor brku zhing
stong pa rmi lam sgyu ma dang mtshungs 'jig rten na
yid la smon pa yis kyang rmongs par byed pa ste
mi yi sems ni bdag nyid gnas pa smos ci 'tshal BCt_11.9

kye ma 'dod pas zil gyis non na mtho ris su
mde ba thob min 'chi ba'i 'jig rten na smos ci
rlung grogs ldan pa'i me yi bud shing gis ji ltar
sred dang bcas pa'i 'dod pa rnams kyis tshim pa med BCt_11.10

'gro na 'dod pa rnams dang mnyam pa'i don med med
rmongs las de rnams khi nar skye bo rab tu chags
de nyid shes nas de ltar don med 'jigs pa ste
shes ldan su zhig rang gis don med mngon par 'dod BCt_11.11

rgya mtsho'i gos can sa ni kun nas thob nas kyang
rgya mtsho chen po'i pha rol rgyal bar 'dod pa ste
rgya mtsho'i chu bo rnams dang chu bran rnams kyis ltar
'jig rten pa yi 'dod pa rnams kyis ngoms pa med BCt_11.12

lha yis gser gyi char pa dag kyang phab gyur la
gling rnams bzhi po mtha' dag la yang longs spyad de
brgya byin gyi yang gdan phyed dag kyang rab thob nas
nga la nu ni yul rnams dag la ngoms pa med BCt_11.13

lha na lha rnams kyi yang rgyal srid longs spyad nas
mchod sbyin brgya ba lha min 'jigs las rab nyams tshe
rgyags las drang srong chen po rnams la'ang khur bcol nas
'dod pa rnams la ngoms med sgra med lhung bar gyur BCt_11.14

e la'i rgyal pos mtho ris rnams ni rnam dkrugs te
brla mdzes lha mo de nyid dbang du byas nas kyang
sred phir drang srong rnams la gser dag phrogs pa ste
yul rnams la ni ngoms med nyams par song bar gyur BCt_11.15

lha min las ni dbang chen dbang chen las sgra med
sgra med las slar dbang chen gang du nyer song ste
mtho ris dang ni sa 'am yul ni de rnams su
skal ba'i tshogs 'khrugs rnams la su zhig blo gtad byed BCt_11.16

shing shun gos can rtsi ba 'bras bu chu za zhing
lag 'gro'i sbrul ltar ring ba'i ral pa'i khur rnams kyang
gang gis don gzhan ma yin thub pa yang nyams te
'dod pa zhes bya'i dgra bo rnams ni su yis 'tshol BCt_11.17

rno ba'i mtshin cha dang ni rno 'dzin mtshon cha yang
gang gi don du 'jigs sde las ni 'chi thob la
de dag rnams kyi dge min sems kyang spyod rnams kyi
'joms phyir de phyir brtul zhugs rnams kyi smos ci dgos BCt_11.18

yul rnams su ni mya ngan nyung ngur shes gyur nas
ku nas sbyor zhing mchog tu ngoms pa med pa nyid
dam pa rnams kyis smod cing nges par sdig pa ste
'dod pa'i ming can dug ni su yis len par byed BCt_11.19

zhing gi las la sogs pa rnams kyis nyam thag cing
'dod pa rnams la mi 'chang rnams kyi rang gnas dang
'dod pa'i bdag nyid rnams kyi rang gnas thos nas ni
'dod pa rnams ni spong bar sems ldan rnams kyis nus BCt_11.20

grub 'gyur 'dod pa rnams su rgyags pa nyer thob phyir
'dod pa can la 'dod 'byor rgud pa shes bya ste
rgyags las bya ba min byed bya ba ma yin la
gang gis zad cing ngan 'gror nye bar 'gro bar 'gyur BCt_11.21

gang las 'bad pas thob cing yongs su bskyabs pa rnams
rnam par bslus nas slar yang so sor 'gro ba ste
bdag nyid ldan pas g.yar po dang mtshungs de rnams su
'dod pa rnams la 'di na mkhas pa su zhig dga' BCt_11.22

btsal nas dang ni blangs nas skom pa skyes pa yis
gang rnams mi 'dor sdug bsngal bar ni yongs 'gro la
'jig rten dag na rtswa sgron dang mtshungs de rnams su
'dod pa rnams la sems ldan su yi dga' ba yin BCt_11.23

bdag ldan min pa snying la gang gis rnam rmugs te
rnam par nyams par 'gro 'gyur bde bar 'gro min zhing
kun nas 'khros pa'i sbrul dang rab mtshungs de rnams su
'dod pa rnams la sems ldan su yi dga' ba yin BCt_11.24

ltogs pas nyam thag kyis bzhin rus pa zos nas kyang
gang rnams la ni ngoms par 'gyur ba ma yin nyid
'khogs pa'i rus pa'i keng rus dang mnyam de rnams su
'dod pa rnams la sems ldan su yi dga' ba yin BCt_11.25

gang gis rgyal po rkun po chu dang me rnams las
thun mong gyur pa nyid phyir sdug bsngal skyed byed de
rab tu gtor ba'i sha dang mtshungs pa de rnams su
'dod pa rnams la sems ldan su yi dga' ba yin BCt_11.26

dgra bo dang ni gnyen 'dun 'brel pa rnams las kyang
gang la gnas pa rnams ni skyen par rgud pa ste
skye mched dang mtshungs nye bar 'tshe ba de rnams su
'dod pa rnams la sems ldan su yi dga' ba yin BCt_11.27

ri dang nags dang chu dang rgya mtsho rnams su yang
gang la rnam par 'phyo ba rnams ni lhung 'gyur te
ldon shing rtse mo'i 'bras bu dang mtshungs de rnams su
'dod la rnams la sems ldan su yi dga' ba yin BCt_11.28

rnam pa sna tshogs 'bad pa drag po 'thob pa rnams
gang gis skad cig gis 'dir nyams par 'gyur ba ste
rmi lam nye bar longs spyod dang mtshungs de rnams su
'dod pa rnams la sems ldan su yi dga' ba yin BCt_11.29

gang rnams bsgrubs nas dang ni rnam par spel nas dang
yongs su bskyabs nas kyang ni bde bar 'gro min la
lci ba'i me ma mir dang rab mtshungs de rnams su
'dod pa rnams la sems ldan su yi dga' ba yin BCt_11.30

gang gi don du sgra ngan rnams ni nyams gyur la
[.. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. ]
ro bsregs shing dang rab tu mtshungs pa de rnams su
'dod pa rnams la bdag ldan su yi dga' ba yin BCt_11.31

lha min mdzes sbyin dang ni nye ba'i mdzes sbyin dag
gang gi don du phan tshun dgrar song nyams gyur la
mdza' bshes gyur cing rnam par 'bral ba de rnams su
'dod pa rnams la sems ldan su yi dga' ba yin BCt_11.32

gang dag rnams kyi don du chu dang me la dang
sha za rnams la bdag nyid 'dir ni 'dor ba ste
dge ba ma yin dgra bor gyur pa de rnams su
'dod pa rnams la sems ldan su yi dga' ba yin BCt_11.33

bshes med 'dod pa'i don du bkren por byed pa ste
gsod dang 'ching ba la sogs sdug bsngal rab thob la
'dod pa'i don du sems ni bkren pa'i dka' thub can
gson pa'i 'jig rten 'ching ba dang ni ngal bar 'gro BCt_11.34

ri dags rnams ni gsod phyir glu yis 'phrog byed la
gzugs kyi don du phye ma leb rnams mer mchong zhing
sha dag don gnyer nya yis lcags ni za ba ste
de phyir yul rnams don med nyid du 'bras bu smin BCt_11.35

'dod pa'i longs spyod yin zhes gang gi blo yin la
kha cig longs spyod rnams ni yongs su spyod pa ste
gos sogs rdzas kyi yon tan yin phyir 'jig rten na
sdug bsngal zhi bar byed ces rab tu gzung bar bya BCt_11.36

skom pa rab tu zhi phyir chu dag 'dod pa ste
bkres pa rnam par nyams phyir bza' ba de bzhin du
rlung dang gdung ba sgrib pa'i ched du khang pa ste
'doms dang grang ba sgrib pa'i phyir ni bgo ba 'o BCt_11.37

de bzhin gnyid ni rnam par 'joms phyir gnas yin la
de bzhin lam la ngal ba nyams phyir theg pa ste
de bzhin gnas ni rnam par spyong phyir stan yin la
gtsang dang nad med stobs la brten phyir khrus yin no BCt_11.38

sdug bsngal rab tu zhi ba'i ched du gyur pa ste
de bzhin skye dag rnams kyi yul rnams longs spyod min
rab tu zhi ba'i cho gar rab zhugs shes rab can
longs spyod rnams ni bza' zhes su yis khas len byed BCt_11.39

gang zhig 'gro ba'i gdung bas rnam par gdungs pa yin
longs spyod yin zhes grang ba'i bya bar nan tan byed
sdug bsngal zhi ba'i bdag nyid la ni rab 'jug cing
des ni 'dod pa rnams la longs spyod 'du shes byed BCt_11.40

gang phyir 'dod pa rnams la mtha' gcig gyur min te
de phyir bdag gi de la longs spyod 'du shes med
dngos po gang nyid kyis ni bde ba ster byed pa
de nyid kyis ni slar yang sdug bsngal 'dren par byed BCt_11.41

bgo ba lci mo dang ni lci ba ma yin nyid
grang dang dro ba'i tshe na bde dang bde min la
zla 'od rnams dang tsan dan nyid dang dro ba na
bde ba'i phyir dang sdug bsngal phyir yin grang ba na'o BCt_11.42

gang phyir rnyed dang ma rnyed la sogs 'jig rten na
kun gyi gnyis su 'dzin pa rnams ni rab zhugs te
de phyir mtha' gcig bde ba yod pa ma yin zhing
sa na skyes bu kha cig mtha' cig sdug bsngal min BCt_11.43

bde dang sdug bsngal nyid ni rnam par 'dres mthong nas
rgyal srid dang ni bran nyid mnyam pa bdag gi lugs
rgyal po nyid ni rtag par rgod pa ma yin zhing
bran ni kun nas gdung ba nyid kyang ma yin no BCt_11.44

gang phyir mi skyong nyid du bka' lung lhag pat gyur
de phyir rgyal po'i sdug bsngal dag ni chen po nyid
kun nas bsten pa'i shing dang rab mtshungs rgyal po ni
srid pa'i rgyu las yongs su ngal bar 'gro ba nyid BCt_11.45

rgyal srid 'dor ldan bshes min mang por mi skyong gis
gal te blo gtad 'cha' bar gyur na rgud pa ste
ci ste yang na blo gtad nye bar byed min na
'dir ni 'jigs ldan rgyal po'i bde ba zhes bya ci BCt_11.46

gang tshe sa ni mtha' dag rgyal bar gyur nas kyang
gnas pa'i ched du grong khyer gcig pi nyid mthong zhing
de nyid la yang pho brang gcig pu bsnyen bya ste
rgyal por gyur pa pha rol don di ngal lam ci BCt_11.47

rgyal po sdod pa'i gnas kyang gnya' shing gcig nyid de
de bzhin bkres pa 'gegs phyir bza' ba tsam yin la
de bzhin nyal lam gcig dang stan ni gcig nyid de
lhag dang lhag min mi mi skyong gi ni rgyags phyir ro BCt_11.48

gal te tshim pa'i don du 'bras bu de 'dod na
rgyal srid rnams dang bral yang bdag ni tshim pa yod
tshim pa yod par gyur na skyes bu'i 'jig rten na
khyad par med pa ma yin thams cad khyad par ro BCt_11.49

de phyir dge dang zhi ba'i lam ni rab thob pa
kho bo 'dod pa rnams la bslu bya ma yin la
mdza' bshes nyid du dran par byas nas yang dang yang
dan bca' nges par skyong zhes bdag la smras pa 'o BCt_11.50

bdag ni nags su zhugs pa mi bzod pas min la
dgra bo'i mda' rnams kyis ni mgo bo 'dar ba min
'bras bu lhag pa rnams las re ba byas min te
de phyir khyed kyi tshig de bzung ba ma yin no BCt_11.51

gang zhig yang yang shin tu sos 'debs khros pa'i sbrul
spangs nas slar yang len pa la ni nan tan byed
yang na sreg pa'i rang bzhin 'bar ba'i rtswa yi me
spangs nas 'dod pa rnams ni slar yang de yis brten BCt_11.52

gang zhig ma long long ba'i phyir ni 'dod pa ste
grol ba 'ching ba'i phyir dang phyug po nor med phyir
rang bzhin gnas pa'i sems ni bsnyen pa'i sems phyir la
yul gyi bdag nyid phyir ni 'dod par de yis byed BCt_11.53

gang zhing 'dir ni mchog tu zhi ba'i bde ba dang
gzhan du sdug bsngal rnams ni kun nas sgrib pa ste
byed ldan rga dang 'chi ba'i 'jigs las sgrol 'dod pa
slongs mo nye bar rgyu zhes rjes su brtse bya min BCt_11.54

gang zhig 'dir ni zhi ba'i bde ba 'thob min la
gzhan du sdug bsngal rnams kyis rab tu 'dzin byed cing
phun tshogs chen po'i bar nyid la yang rnam gnas pa'i
sred pa zil gyis non la rjes su brtse bar bya BCt_11.55

sems dpa' yi dang spyod pa yi dang rigs nyid kyi
khyod kyi brjod pa la ni rjes su mthun pa ste
sems dpa' yi dang spyod pa yi dang rigs nyid kyi
kho bo yi yang dam bca' 'dren par mtshungs pa 'o BCt_11.56

bdag kyang 'khor ba'i mda' yis rnam phug pa
zhi ba thob par 'dod pas rnam par nges 'byung ste
nad med mtho ris na yang rgyal srid 'thob pa ru
'dod pa med na kye ma mi rnams su smod ci BCt_11.57

mi skyong gang yang ste gsum mtha' dag brten pa 'di
rab mchog mi yi don zhes khyed kyis bdag la smras
de ltar don med ces ni bdag gi brten pa 'dir
'dzad ldan sde mtshan gsum ni tshim byed kyang ma yin BCt_11.58

gang du rga bar 'gro min 'jigs min nad ma yin
skye min nye bar 'da' min sems kyi nad rnams min
gang na yang dag yang du bya ba yod min pa
de nyid skyes bu'i don ni mchog tu shes pa 'o BCt_11.59

ji srid na tshod so ma rnam par 'gyur bar 'gro
de srid rga ba yongs si skyongs mdzod zhes smras pa
'di ni nges pa ma yin g.yo bar mthong ba ste
rga ba brtan pa min dang lang tsho brtan ldan mthong BCt_11.60

rang gi las mkhan mthar byed gang gis 'gro ba ni
na tshod kun ka dbang med rnam par 'gugs pa ste
rnam bzhag ma yin rnam par nyams tshe gang ltar ni
zhi 'dod mkhas pa dag gis rga ba rtogs par byed BCt_11.61

gang tshe rga ba'i gzhi dang nad rnam bkram pa'i mda'
mthar byed dge ba ma yin rngon pa bzhin gnas pas
skye dgu'i ri dags skal ba'i nags rten rnams gtor te
na tshod rab mchog la dmigs yid la re ba ci BCt_11.62

de phyir gzhon nam rgan dang yang na byis pa ni
rab tu 'jug par 'dod dam rnam par ldog pa nyid
chos ldan bdag nyid byas pa ji lta bar gyur pa
de ltar myur ba ldan pas 'dir ni bya bar 'os BCt_11.63

yang na 'dod pa'i bras bu rigs su 'os pa rnams
chos phyir mchod sbyin bya ba gyis zhes gang smras pa
gang zhig gzhan gyi sdug bsngal bya bas 'dod pa ste
mchod sbyin rnams la phyag 'tshal bde ba 'dod pa med BCt_11.64

'bras nu 'dod pas dbang med pha rol gsod pa la
snying rje'i bdag nyid dam pa rnams kyi rigs tshul min
gang yang mchod sbyin dag gi 'bras bu rtag gyur pa
snying rje'i bdag nyid gang gi deltar byas nas ci BCt_11.65

sems ni zhi ba yis sam tshul khrims brtul zhugs kyis
gal te chos tshul gzhan gyi cha ga ma yin la
de lta na yang mchod sbyin bsnyen par 'os min te
gang du gzhan la 'tshes nas 'bras bur brjod pa 'o BCt_11.66

'di nyid du yang re zhig skyes bu gnas pa yi
bde ba gang zhig pha rol 'tshe bas rab zhugs pa
de yang brtse bcas blo dang ldan pa'i 'do min te
gang zhig srid pa'i tha mar mi mthong kye ma ci BCt_11.67

rgyal po 'khor bar bdag gi yid ni dga' med cing
'bras bur rab tu 'jug phyir bdag ni bslu bya min
chu 'dzin char gyis brgyab pa'i ljon shing bzhin du ni
kun tu song ba'i rab tu 'jug pa rnams ni g.yo BCt_11.68

rnam par thar ba smra ldan rtsibs 'phur thub pa ni
blta bar 'dod pas bdag ni 'dir yongs de yi phyir
mi skyong khyod la dge bar gyur cig da ni 'gro
bdag gi de nyid ltos med ngag ni bzod par mdzod BCt_11.69

lha na dbang po bzhin bsrungs rtag par nyi bzhin bsrungs
yon tan gyis bsrungs sa bsrungs 'dir ni dge legs bsrungs
tshe bsrungs 'phags pa yis bsrungs dam pa'i bu rnams dang
dpal bsrungs rgyal po bdag nyid kyi ni chos bsrungs shig BCt_11.70

kha ba'i dgra yi tog las skyes pa las skyes nas
ji ltar gnyis gang zhig lus ni rnam thar 'gro
kha ba'i dgra yi dgra yis khyim gyi dgra 'joms nang
nang du de ltar gang zhig yid ni rnam par thar gshegs mdzod BCt_11.71

thal mo sbyar bcas te thob mi skyongs gis smras pa
khyed kyis ji ltar 'dod pa gegs med thob par shog
bya ba byas pa kun nas thob pa dus su 'dod
kho bo yi yang rjes su 'dzin pa khyed kyis mdzad pa 'o BCt_11.72

de ltar gyur zhes brtan pa'i dam bca' mdzad nas sa skyong la
de nas de ni thams cad sgrol gyi dka' thub gnas su gshegs
yongs su gshegs pa de mthong nas kyang ngo mtshar gyur pa yi
myi skyong nyid kyang ri yi tshogs kyi grong khyer nyid du song BCt_11.73

| sangs rgyas kyi spyod pa zhes bya ba'i snyan dngags chen po las | chen po las 'dod pa la rnam par smod pa'i le'u ste bcu gcig pa'o ||

de nas lus kyis gang ba bzhin
bu ram shing pa'i zla ba yis
zhi bar gnas pa'i thub pa yiyi
rtsibs 'phur gyigyi corr. ni gnas su bsnyen BCt_12.1

sgyu rtsal shes kyi rigs de yis
rgyang nas gzigs nas mthon po yis
legs par 'ongs zhes smras pa ste
drung du nye bar gshegs pa'o BCt_12.2

de gnyis phan tshun rigs par ni
khams ni snyoms par dris nas su
shing gtsang brtul zhugs gdan dag la
sa phyogs gtsang bar bzhugs pa'o BCt_12.3

bkur mang rnam par yangs pa yi
lta byed dag gis 'thung ba bzhin
mi skyong sras po bzhugs de la
thub pa mchog des smras pa'o BCt_12.4

zhi ba bdag gis shes pa ltar
khyim nas nges par byung bar gyur
gnyis 'thung rgyags pas zhags pa ltar
brtse ba'i zhags pa bcad nas 'ongs BCt_12.5

khyod kyi yid ni shes rab dang
kun nas brtan pa ldan pa nyid
dug gi ljon pa'i 'bras bu bzhin
gang khyod dpal dor nas 'ongs so BCt_12.6

longs spyad lhag ma'i phreng ba bzhin
bu rnams dag la dpal byin nas
sa skyong 'khogs pa'i na tshod rnams
gang zhig nags 'ongs ngo mtshar min BCt_12.7

bdag gi lugs ni ngo mtshar te
so ma'i na tshod la khyod kyis
yul gyi spyod yul la gnas pa
dpal nyid longs ma spyad nas 'ongs BCt_12.8

de phyir chos 'di shes pa la
khyod ni dam pa'i snod yin la
ye shes gru bo byin rlabs nas
skyen par sdug bsngal rgya mtsho sgrol BCt_12.9

gang yang slob mar shes pa na
dus kyis bstan bcos la 'jug ste
zab pa las dang nan tan las
bdag gi yongs rtog khyod ma yin BCt_12.10

de ltar rtsibs 'phur nyid kyi tshig
mi yi drang srong des gsan nas
mchog tu dga' bar gyur pa yis
lan gnyis rab tu smras pa'o BCt_12.11

don ma byas kyang 'di yis ni
don byas bzhin du da lta nyid
chags dang bral ba gang 'di ni
dam pa khyed kyi mngon du gyur BCt_12.12

blta bar 'dod pas 'od bzhin dang
sgrol bar 'dod pas gru bzhin dang
'gro bar 'dod pas lam mkhan bzhin
khyed mthong ba las bdag gis shes BCt_12.13

rga dang 'chi ba'i 'jigs rnams las
[.. .. .. .. .. .. .. ]
gal te gsung byar dgongs nas ni
de phyir gsung bar 'os pa'o BCt_12.14

de ltar rtsibs 'phur gyis gzhon nu'i
bdag nyid che las bskul ba nyid
rang nyid kyi ni bstan bcos kyi
nges par mdor bsdus gsungs pa'o BCt_12.15

ji ltar 'khor ba yin pa la
ji ltar nges par ldog pa nyid
nyan pa rnams kyi mchog grub mtha'
kho bo'i 'di ni gson mdzod cig BCt_12.16

rang bzhin dang ni rnam 'gyur dang
skye dang 'chi dang rga ba ste
re zhig sems dpa' zhes brjod pa
brtan pa'i sems dpa' de shes mdzod BCt_12.17

de la rang bzhin shes bya ba
rang bzhin shes pa shes par mdzod
'byung ba lnga yi bdag nyid dang
blo dang mi gsal ba nyid do BCt_12.18

rnam 'gyur zhes bya mkhen par mdzod
yul rnams dang ni dbang po rnams

'di ni zhi ba ma yin 'byung po'i tshogs rnams kyis
'jigs dang bsdigs dang rdeg pa rnams ni 'os pa'o BCt_13.17

de nas bdud kyis rang gi sde ni dran pa ste
shākya thub pa'i bgegs ni mnyam por byed 'dod pa
ral gri be con shing rtse ljon shing rtse gsum mdun lag rnams
sna tshogs bsam pa dang ldan rjes su 'brang rnams 'ongs BCt_13.18

phag dang nya dang bong bu rnga mo'i gdong can rnams
stag dang dom dang seng ge gnyis 'thung gdong can rnams
mig gcig kha ni du ma mgo bo gsum ldan rnams
gsum pa 'phyang ba rnams dang gsus pa che ba rnams BCt_13.19

brla rnams pus mo'i bar du bum pa'i pus mo rnams
mche ba'i mtshon cha rnams dang sen mo'i mtshon cha rnams
keng rus gdong can rnams dang gzugs ni mang po rnams
gdong phyed zhom pa rnams dang gdong ni chen po rnams BCt_13.20

thal skya rnams dang thig le dmar po sna tshogs rnams
kha ṭwāṃ ga rnams dang ni spre'u ltar dud skra rnams
'phreng 'phyang rnams dang glang po'i rna ba'i rna ba rnams
pags pa'i gos can rnams dang gos dang bral ba rnams BCt_13.21

gdong phyed dkar po rnams dang lus phyed ljang khu rnams
zangs mdog dud mdog rnams dang ljang gu dkar po rnams
sbrul gyi sham thabs rnams dang de bzhin lag pa rnams
rab tu sgro sgrogs dril bu 'khrugs pa'i ska rags rnams BCt_13.22

ta la'i tshad mnyam rnams dang mdung rnams bzung ba rnams
byis pa'i tshad mnyam rnams dang mche ba gtsigs pa rnams
lug gi gdong can rnams dang bya yi mig can rnams
byi la'i gdong can rnams dang mi yi lus can rnams BCt_13.23

skra bkam rnams dang ral pa can dang byi bo rnams
gos dmar rnams dang rnam par 'khrugs pas dkris pa rnams
rab dga'i gdong can rnams dang gnyer ma'i gdong can rnams
gzi brjid 'phrog pa rnams dang yid ni 'phrog pa rnams BCt_13.24

kha cig dag ni 'gro zhing drang tu phan tshun du
mchan khung 'khyud cing de bzhin gzhan rnams mchongs
mkha' la 'gro ba rnams ni kha cig rtse ba ste
kha cig shing gi rtse mo rnams la zhon pa'o BCt_13.25

kha cig rtse gsum skor zhing gar ni byed pa ste
kha cig dbyug pa gdengs shing thog sgra sgrogs pa'o
kha cig dga' bas khyu mchog bzhin du skad 'don zhing
kha cig lus 'phros rnams las rab tu 'bar bar gyur BCt_13.26

'dzin par 'dod pa rnams dang 'joms par 'dod pa rnams
jo bo'i bka' ni rab tu skyong bar byed pa ste
rnam pa de ltar 'byung po'i tshogs rnams kun nas ni
byang chub sems dpa' de la yongs su bskor nas gnas BCt_13.27

mtshan mo snga ma la ni shākya'i khyu mchog dang
bdud kyi 'thab mo dus de rab tu mthong nas ni
nam mkha' gsal ba ma yin sa ni g.yos gyur la
phyogs rnams sgra dang bcas pa rab tu 'bar bar gyur BCt_13.28

drag po'i shugs can rlung ni kun tu g.yos gyur la
skar ma rnams ni mi sngan zla ba gsal ma gyur
slar yang mtshan mor mun pa rnam par gyas gyur la
rgya mtsho rnams mi thams cad kun tu g.yos par gyur BCt_13.29

sa gzhi 'dzin cing chos dag 'dzin pa'i klu rnams ni
thub pa chen po'i bgegs la bzod pa ma yin zhing
bdud la khros pas rnam par log pa'i mig can rnams
rngam pa bton zhing lus ni rnam par gyur pa'o BCt_13.30

gtsang mar lhag par gnas pa'i lha yi drang srong ni
dam chos bsrung ba'i don du mngon par zhugs pa rnams
bdud la yid kyis rjes su brtse ba byas pa ste
chags dang bral ba las kyang khros par ma gyur to BCt_13.31

'tshe ba'i bdag nyid bdud kyi dpung ni de yis ni
byang chub rtsa ba de ni khyab pa mthong nas ni
chos kyi bdag nyid 'jig rten thar pa 'dod rnams kyis
nam mkha' dag la ha ha'i sgra dag byas par gyur BCt_13.32

chos kyi cho ga de ni nye bar nyams byed pa
bdud dpung gnas pa drang srong chen pos gzigs nas ni
ba lang rnams kyi dbus su seng ge gnas pa bzhin
g.yo 'gul med cing rnam par 'gyur bar yang ma gyur BCt_13.33

de nas de yi 'jigs pa'i ched du bdud kyis ni
'byung po'i sde ni drang ba rnams la bka' stsal cing
de nas 'di yi sde des rang rang mthu rnams kyis
de yi brtan pa dbye phyir blo gros byas pa'o BCt_13.34

kha cig lce rnams g.yo zhing du mas rnam 'chang zhing
mche ba'i rtse mo rnams rno mig rnams ljang ser zlum
kha rnams gdangs shing phur bu'i rna ba rnams brtan cing
kun nas skrag par byed pa snyam du gnas zhes grags BCt_13.35

des ni gzugs dang bsam pa dag gis mi bzad pa
rnam pa de lta nyid du gnas pa de rnams las
rtsod mo byed pa'i byis pa rgyags pa rnams las ni
drang srong chen po zug med skyo bar ma gyur to BCt_13.36

de nas kha cig khros pas lta byed rnam 'gyur zhing
'di la dbyug pa brdeg par 'bad pa bya ba ste
sngon tshe grong khyer 'joms pa'i rdo rje dang bcas ltar
de nas 'di yi dbyug pa dang bcas lag pa rengs BCt_13.37

kha cig rdo dang shing rnams gyen du 'phyar ba ni

'bigs byed ri brag rnams ni rdo rje bcom pa bzhin

kha cig mkha' la gyen du 'phur bas rdo rnams dang

kha dog gcig min mtshams sprin rkang pa rnams bzhin du
mngon par lhung ba ma yin rnam par gnas par gyur BCt_13.39

ngzan ni de yi steng du 'bar ba'i khyu mchog gi
glang po ri bo tsam pa'i rwa can 'phangs pa ste
de ni 'phangs pa tsam na nam mkhar gnas pa nyid
de yi mthu las rnam pa brgyar ni gas par gyur BCt_13.40

'jig rten 'jig tshe lhun po rab tu 'bar ba yis
gser gyi bya skyibs rnams kyi phye ma rnams bzhin du

me mdag char pa chen po mkha' las phab par gyur BCt_13.41

byang chub shing gi rtsa bar rab tu rnam 'phangs pa'i
me stag 'phro ba dang bcas me mdag char pa de
drang srong rnam pa mchog gi byams pa'i gnas pa las
u tpa la dmar po'i 'dab ma'i char par gyur pa'o BCt_13.42

lus dang sems la rnam par gnod par bya ba'i phyir

rang gi nges pa'i gnyen 'dun nye bar 'khyud nas bzhin
shākya thub pa gdan las g.yos par ma gyur to BCt_13.43

de nas gzhan rnams 'khogs pa'i ljon shing rnams nas ltar
kha rnams las ni sbrul rnams rnam par skyugs pa ste
sngags kyis bcings bzhin de rnams de yi drang du ni
song ba ma yin dbugs min g.yos par ma gyur to BCt_13.44

gzhan rnams glog dang bcas shing thog dang bcas pa yis
chu 'dzin chen po gtum pa'i dbyangs ldan rnams gyur nas
ljon shing de la rdo ba'i char pa phab pa ste
de ni me tog char pa mdzes par gyur pa'o BCt_13.45

dbang phyug ma yin sron par dka' ba'i mi yi na
snying la yongs su g.yos pa'i khro ba bzhin du ni
de nas gzhan gyis gzhu la mda' dag bkod pa ni
de nyid du ni 'bar zhing lhung bar ma gyur to BCt_13.46

yul la rab tu 'jug la 'khor ba la 'jigs pa
yongs su rtog pa po yi dbang po lnga rnams bzhin
ngzan rnams dag gis mda' lnga rab tu 'phangs pa rnams
nam mkha' gnas shing thub pa la ni ma lhung ngo BCt_13.47

gzhan ni brdeg par 'dod pas khros shing rab bskor zhing
dbyug pa bzung nas drang srong chen po'i mngon du phyogs
don med byed pa'i nyes pa rnams la 'jig rten bzhin
des ni 'dod pa ma thob dbang med 'gyel bar gyur BCt_13.48

bud med sprin pa nag po lag na thod pa can
drang srong chen po'i thugs ni rmongs par byed ces grags
g.yoba'i bdag nyid can gyi blo ni lung la bzhin
der ni nges par med par skor zhing gnas ma yin BCt_13.49

kha cig mig ni rab tu 'bar bar byas nas ni
mig gi me yis sbrul gyi dug bzhin bsreg 'dod pas
'dod pa'i bdag nyid can gyis nyer gnas dpal bzhin du
der ni drang srong bzhugs pa mthong bar ma gyur to BCt_13.50

ye shes ting 'dzin dag gis 'gro bya nye legs chos
lus kyi ngal ba rnams kyis 'thob par 'dod pa bzhin
de bzhin gzhan ni rdo ba lci mo bteg pa ni
rab tu 'bad pa rnam bcom don med ngal bar gyur BCt_13.51

de bzhin gzhan rnams dred dang seng ge'i rnam pa yis
chen po'i sgra rnams mthon por rab tu sgrogs pa ste
rdo rjes bsnun pa'i nam mkha' lags pa zhes snyam nas
sems can rnams ni gang gis kun nas 'khums par gyur BCt_13.52

ri dags glang po rnams ni nyam thag skad 'don zhing
rnam par 'bros shing 'thig pa nyid du gyur pa ste
de yi mtshan mor phyogs rnams las ni nyin mo bzhin
nyam thag bya rnams skad 'don yongs su babs par gyur BCt_13.53

rnam pa de ltar de rnams kyi sgra de rnams kyis
'byung po thams cas rnams su g.yos pa yin na yang
khwa rnams dag gi sgra rnams dag gis mkha' lding ltar
thub pa 'jigs pa ma yin 'khums par ma gyur to BCt_13.54

'jigs pa 'dren pa yongs su bskor ba'i tshogs rnams las
ji ltar ji ltar thub pa'i 'jigs pa ma yin pa
de ltar de ltar chos 'dzin rnams kyi dgra bo yi
bdud rnams mya ngan las dang khros nas byer ba'o BCt_13.55

de nas 'byung po cung zhig gzugs ni mthong min zhing
khyad par 'phags par gyur pa nam mkhar gnas nyid kyis
drang srong la gnod dgra ma yin la khros mthong nas
bdud lha chen po'i dbyangs kyis smras par gyur pa'o BCt_13.56

don med ngal bar byed par 'os pa ma yin bdud
'tshe ba'i bdag nyid spong la bde bar song mdzod dang
ri bo chen po lhun po rlung rnams kyis bzhin du
khyod kyis bskyod cing bsgul bar nus pa ma yin no BCt_13.57

sa yis brtan pa nyid dang chu yis gsher ba nyid
me yis dro ba nyid ni rab tu 'dor ba yang
bskal pa du mar bslab pa'i bsod nams las mnga' ba
'dis ni nan tan nges par 'dor ba ma yin no BCt_13.58

'di yi nges pa gang dang pha rol gnon pa dang
gzi brjid gang dang brtse ba skye dgu rnams la ste
'od zer stong gis mun rnams ma bcom gnas bzhin du
'di ni de nyid ma thob nas ni ldang ma yin BCt_13.59

shing la bsrubs na me ni rnyed par 'gyur ba ste
sa la brkos na chu yang 'thob par 'gyur ba nyid
rigs pa dang ni ldan pa'i thams cad byas pa ste
brtson 'grus ldan pa'i bsgrub bya ma yin ci yang med BCt_13.60

de phyir chags sogs nad rnams dag la gnas pa yi
'jig rten nyam thag pa la thugs rje mnga' ba ni
ye shes sman gyi don du yongs su ngal ba po
sman pa chen po 'di la bgegs 'os ma yin no BCt_13.61

lam ngan mang po rnams kyis 'jig rten stor ba la
gang zhig zhi bas dam pa'i lam ni rjes tshol ba
chud zos pa la legs par ston byed ded dpon bzhin
ston mdzad de ni bskyod par rigs pa ma yin no BCt_13.62

mun pa chen po sems can chud zos rnams la ni
ye shes sgron ma rab tu gsal bar mdzad pa 'di
mun pa la ni rab tu 'bar ba'i sgron ma bzhin
'phags pa'i mya ngan 'da' bar byed par 'os ma yin BCt_13.63

'khor ba'i rnam 'gyur chu bo chen por 'gro ba ni
pha rol ma thob par ni bying bar gzigs nas ni
gang gis de ni sgrol bar byed la rab zhugs te
de la sdig pa 'phags pa su yis sems par byed BCt_13.64

bzod pa'i chu rgyus brtan pa'i rtsa ba brtan pa ste
spyod pa'i me tog blo dang dran pa'i yal ga can
ye shes ljon shing chos kyi 'bras bu ster ba po
'phel bzhin pa ni zlog par 'os pa ma yin no BCt_13.65

gang gis snying la rmongs pa'i zhags pa sra rnams kyis
bcings pa'i skye dgu rnams kyi grol phyir blo mnga' zhing
'gro ba bcings pa thar pa'i ched du 'o brgyal ba
de la brdeg pa khyed kyi 'thad pa ma yin no BCt_13.66

byang chub ched du las gang dag ni mdzad pa rnams
de rnams kyi ni nges par de ring dus yin la
ji ltar thub pa snga ma rnams ni de bzhin du
gnas der de bzhin 'di ni nye bar bzhugs pa'o BCt_13.67

dbyig 'dzin sa gzhi yi ni lte ba 'di yin zhing
snying po dam pa mtha' dag dang ni ldan pa nyid
gang zhig 'di yi ting nge 'dzin gyi shugs bzod pa'i
sa yi phyogs de 'di las gzhan pa yod ma yin BCt_13.68

de phyir khro bar ma byed zhi bar nyer song la
bdud ni khyod kyi dregs pas nga rgyal ma gyur cig
dpal ni mi brtan blo gtad par ni nus min zhing
go 'phang g.yo la rgyags par mngon par nyer 'gro ci BCt_13.69

de nas de yi tshig de yang dag thos nas kyang
thub pa chen po'i g.yo ba med pa nyid mthong nas
gang gi mda' yis 'gro ba'i snying la rdeg byed pa'i
bdud ni 'bad pa bcom zhing yid mi bde bar song BCt_13.70

dga' ba med cing 'bras med ngal ba byas pa rnams
pha ong rnams ni khyu mchog ljon shing rnams gtor te
dgrar gyur dgra bo'i dpung ni gtso bo bsad pa ltar
de nas 'di yi dpung ni phyogs phyogs bros pa'o BCt_13.71

me tog tog can 'khor dang bcas pa bros shing nges par 'pham pa na
drang srong chen po mun pa 'pham zhing rdul dang bral ba rgyal ba na
rgod pa dang bcas lang tsho ma bzhin zla ba dang bcas | mkha' gsal zhing
chu'i snying po can gyi dri zhes me tog char pa bab par gyur pa'o BCt_13.72

de ltar sdig pa can ni nges par pham pa na
de tshe phyogs ni rab snang mtshan mor byed pa mdzes
mkha' las me tog char rnams sa la bab pa ste
lang tsho mo bzhin ngal ba med par mtshan mo gsal BCt_13.73

| sangs rgyas kyi spyod pa zhes bya ba'i snyan dngags chen po las | bdud las rnam par rgyal ba'i le'u ste | bcu gsum pa'o ||

| de nas brtan dang zhi ba yis
bdud kyi stobs ni pham mdzad nas
don dam rnam par mkhyen bzhed pa
bsam gtan mkhas de bsam gtan mdzad BCt_14.1

bsam gtan cho ga thams cad la
dbang phyug dam pa rab brnyes nas
sngon gyi skye ba rim pa ni
dang po'i thun la dran pa'o BCt_14.2

che ge mo bdag ming 'di ni
de nas 'phos te 'dir 'ongs pa'o
zhes ni skye ba stong phrag rnams
rjes su myong ba bzhin du dran BCt_14.3

'thad pa de dang de rnams su
skye ba 'chi ba dran nas ni
de nas sems can la thugs rje
thugs rje'i bdag nyid can gyis mdzad BCt_14.4

rang gi skye bo bor nas ni
slar yang gzhan du bya ba rnams
nges par 'jig rten mgon med 'di
'khor lo bzhin du yongs su 'khor BCt_14.5

de ltar nges pa'i bdag nyid ni
de yi dran pa'i gyur pa ste
chi shing snying po snying po med
'khor ba de ltar nges par ro BCt_14.6

thun ni gnyis pa byung ba na
gnyis med pha rol gnon pa de
mig dang ldan pa kun gyi mchog
lha yi spyan ni thob par gyur BCt_14.7

de nas des ni lha yi spyan
yongs su dag pa de yis ni
me long dri ma med pa ltar
'jig rten mtha' dag la gzigs so BCt_14.8

mchog dag mchog min las rnams kyi
sems can rnams kyi 'chi 'pho dang
skye ba gzigs pa de yi ni
thugs rje'i bdag nyid 'phel bar gyur BCt_14.9

'di rnams sdig pa'i las can rnams
srog chags rnams ni ngan 'gror 'gro
'di gzhan dge ba'i las can rnams
mtho ris su ni rab gnas so BCt_14.10

shin tu mi bzad dmyal ba ru
rab tu 'jigs par gyur pa rnams
'di rnams sdug bsngal sna tshogs kyis
kye ma bkren par bcer bar byed BCt_14.11

kha cig me yi kha dog gi
lcags khu khol ma 'thung bar byed

gzhan rnams cho nges 'debs shing 'dzegs BCt_14.12

lcags zangs rnams su khas bub rnams

me mdag phung po 'bar rnams su
kha cig snying rje rab sreg go BCt_14.13

kha cig lcags kyi mche rno can
mi bzad khyi rnams kyis za zhing

lcags 'dra'i bya rog rnams kyis za BCt_14.14

kha cig gdung bas yongs ngal rnams

'di rnams bcings pa bzhin du zhugs BCt_14.15

sdug bsngal na yang rnam mi smrin BCt_14.16

sdug bsngal bzlog pa'i don ched du
bde ba yin zhes las gang byas
de yi 'bras de dbang med kyis
sdug bsngal kho na nyer longs spyod BCt_14.17

bde don mi dge ba byas nas
gang de shin tu sdug bsngal rnams
de dag rnams kyi ro myang des
bde ba phra ma yang byed dam BCt_14.18

sdig pa'i bdag nyid rgod rnams kyis
sdig pa'i las ni byas pa gang
de ni sngon dun gyur pa'i tshe
cho nge rnams kyis rjes su myong BCt_14.19

gal te de ltar sdig las can
las kyi 'bras bu mthong ba ste
dmig su mngon par bsnun pa bzhin
skyen par khrag ni skyug pa nyid BCt_14.20

lus kyi sdug bsngal rnams las dang
dmyal ba'i rnams las sems ldan gyi
'phags min rnams dang lhan cig 'grogs
ngal ba mchog ni bdag gi lugs BCt_14.21

gzhan 'di sems kyi rnam g.yo las
byung ba'i las rnams sna tshogs kyis
byol song skye gnas sna tshogs su
nye bar skyes rnams gdung ba can BCt_14.22

sha lpags spu dang so yi phyir
chags pa las sam rgyags pa las

gang du snying brje bar gsod do BCt_14.23

nus med ldan yang dbang med rnams
bkres skom ngal bas btsir ba rnams

rta dang ba lang gyur rnams 'khol BCt_14.24

glang por gyur pa rnam 'khol te

rkang pa'i rting pa rnams kyis brdegs BCt_14.25

gzhan gyi dbang du gyur nyid kyis
sdug bsngal gzhan rnams la spyod kyang
gang la sdug bsngal khyad par ldan BCt_14.26

phan tshun du ni rab phrad nas
skam gnas skam gnas rnams kyis dang
chur gnas chur gnas rnams kyis dang
mkhar gnas mkhar gnas rnams kyis 'joms BCt_14.27

ser snas non pa'i sems ldan rnams
yi dags 'jig rten snang med du
skyes pa 'di rnams de bzhin du
bkren pa 'bras bu la longs spyod BCt_14.28

khab mig lta bu'i kha rnams dang
ri bo lta bu'i lto ba rnams
bkres skom gyis bskyed sdug bsngal gyis
sdug bsngal skal can rnams btsir to BCt_14.29

ser sna'i 'bras bu 'di 'dra ba
skyes bus gal te shes na ni

zhi ba bzhin du kun nas gtong BCt_14.30

rang gi las rnams kyis bzung zhing
sred pas shin tu non pa rnams

longs spyod par ni 'did mi rnyed BCt_14.31

'di gzhan dmyal ba dang mtshungs pa'i

nye bar skyes rnams mi rnams su
'gro ba rnams ni sdug bsngal 'thob BCt_14.32

de sngon skye ba tsam na yang
lag pa rnon pos bzung ba rnams
ral gri rnams kyis gshegs pa ltar
gang du snying rje bar ni ngu BCt_14.33

byams dang bsrung dang skyong rnams kyis

rang rang las kyis nyon mongs so BCt_14.34

zhes ni gang du lhag par la

'di gzhan bsod nams las rnams kyis

me ltar rab tu sreg par byed BCt_14.36

gyen du mig phyogs rnam lhung ngo BCt_14.37

gang du lha mo rnams kyis ni

lag pa rnams kyis gos rnams 'dzin BCt_14.38

gang zhig sa la ltung ba bzhin
lung 'dod do shal g.yo rnams kyis
sdug rnams gzhal med khang rnams nas
snying rje dang bcas ltung la lta BCt_14.39

rnam pa sna tshogs rgyan phreng can
gzhan 'did sdug bsngal lhung rnams la

lta byed rnams kyis rjes su 'gro BCt_14.40

'dod pa can rnams lhung ba la

'khrugs chen gyis ltar nyam thag pa
lha mo'i tshogs rnams kyis brten to BCt_14.41

kyi hud shing rta sna tshogs rdzing
kyi hud sdug pa gang na zhes
nyam thag pa rnams rnam zlos shing

|| zhi zhing mdangs ldan mdzad pa kun nas brnyes pa de

ji ltar skam po'i rten la gnas pa'i rlung gis ni
bus pa'i me yi zhi ba yod pa ma yin no
de bzhin 'dod pa'i rten la gnas pa'i chags pa yis
rjes su song ba'i sems kyi zhi ba yod ma min BCt_15.33

mtha' 'di gnyis pa dag kyang rnam par dor byas nas
bdag gis lam gzhan dbu mas lhag par rtogs pa ste
shin tu sdig bsngal nye bar zhi ba'i 'dren pa'o
bde ba dang ni dge ba nyid dang bral ba'o BCt_15.34

yang dag lta ba'i nyi mas rab tu gsal byas shing
rnam dag yang dag rtogs pa'i shing rtas drangs pa ste
yang dag brjod pa'i yang dag ngag ni gtsug lag khang
dge ba'i bya ba'i skyed tshal brgya phrag mngon par dga' BCt_15.35

smad pa med pa'i 'tsho ba lo legs chen po ste
yang dag rtsol bas stobs dang rjes su 'gro ba can
kun tu yang dag dran pa'i sbas pas sbas pa ste
ting 'dzin gzims mal dang ni gdan dang bzhugs pa yis BCt_15.36

de ltar mchog gi yan lag brgyad 'dir 'di lam ste
'chi dang rga dang na ba rnams las 'dren pa'o
gang las drangs nas bya ba thams cad byas pa ste
'di dang che ge mor ni slar yang 'gro ba med BCt_15.37

'di ni sdug bsngal mtha' dag 'di ni mtshan ma ste
'di ni 'gog pa 'di yi lam ni 'di yin te
de ltar ma thos chos kyi cho ga sngar med pa'i
rnam par thar phyir bdag gi spyan mig skyes pa'o BCt_15.38

skye dang rga dang na dang de nas rgud pa dang
sdug pa dang bral mi sdug pa dang sbyor ba dang
'dod pa'i don ni rab tu thob pa med pa ste
rnam pa sna tshogs sdug bsngal 'di ni yongs su 'thob BCt_15.39

'dod pa'i bdag can gyi 'am bdag rgyal can gyi 'am
lus can gyi 'am yang na lus can ma yin pa'i
gang zhig yon tan med pa gang la rab zhugs kyang
mdor bsdus nas de sdug bsngal du ni shes par mdzod BCt_15.40

ji ltar 'bar ba zhi ba'i me ni chung na yang
lhan cig skyes pa dro ba'i ngo bo spong min nyid
de bzhin bdag tu 'du shes zhi sogs kyis phra yang
sdug bsngal bdag nyid can zhes bdag gi shin tu nges BCt_15.41

ji ltar sa chu sa bon dus rnams myu gu'i bzhin
'dod chags la sogs rnam pa sna tshogs skyon rnams dang
skyon las rab tu skyes pa'i las rnams nyid dag ni
sdug bsngal dag gi rgyur ni nges par shes par mdzod BCt_15.42

mtho ris su 'am 'og tu srid pa'i rgyun la ni
'dod chags la sogs skyon gyi tshogs rnams rgyu yin zhing
dman dang 'bring dang mchog ste sna tshogs nyid kyi ni
de dang der ni las rnams dag ni rtsa ba'o BCt_15.43

nyes pa zad las 'khor ba'i rgyu ni yod min te
las zad pa las sdug bsngal de ni yod ma yin
gang phyir don gang yod pa las ni kun 'byung ste
de phyir med pa las de slar yang 'byung ba med BCt_15.44

gang du skye ba med cing rga med 'chi ba med
me med sa med chu med mkha' med rlung med la
thog ma bar dang mtha' med 'phags pa dgrog bya min
dge zhing 'gyur med 'gog pa de ni shes par mdzod BCt_15.45

yan lag brgyad ldan gang zhig mngon brjod de lam ste
lhag par rtogs phyir 'di yi thabs de'i gzhan ma yin
lam 'di yi ni ma mthong ba las 'jig rten rnams
de nyid dang ni nye du rnams ni yongs su 'khor BCt_15.46

sdug bsngal yongs su shes par bya zhing rgyu 'di ni
spang bya 'gog pa yang ni dbang du bya'o
de bzhin lam 'di yang ni bsgom par bya ba ste
de ltar 'dir ni bdag gi blo gros rab zhugs so BCt_15.47

sdug bsngal 'di ni yongs shes rgyu ni spangs pa ste
de bzhin du ni 'gog pa mngon du byas pa'o
de bzhin du ni 'di yi lam 'di bsgoms pa ste
de ltar 'dir ni bdag gi spyan mig rab zhugs so BCt_15.48

ji srid du ni yang dag 'phags pa'i bden pa ni
bzhi pa'i rkang pa 'di rnams mthong ba ma yin pa
de srid bdag 'dir grol ba med par zhes brjod cing
bdag nyid la ni don byas nyid du yang ma mthong BCt_15.49

gang tshe 'phags pa'i bden pa rnams ni rtogs pa ste
rtogs nas kyang ni don byar 'os pa byas pa'o
de tshe bdag nyid rnam par grol zhes brjod pa ste
bdag nyid la ni don byas nyid du yang mthong ngo BCt_15.50

de ltar drang srong chen po thugs rje mnga' ba yi
'dir ni chos dag de skad mngon par gsungs pa na
kau ṇḍi nya'i rigs dang lha ni brgya phrag rnams
gtsang zhing rdul dang bral ba'i mig ni thob par gyur BCt_15.51

bya ba thams cad nges par byas shing zhi ba de la ni
thams cad mkhyen pas khyu mchog bzhin du mthon po'i dbyangs kyis gsungs
khyod kyi ye shes bdag nyid chen pos des ni tshig gsol ba
legs so khyod kyi blo gros mchog ni bdag gis shes pa'o BCt_15.52

legs so bdag gis shes shes de nas des ni 'jig rten ni
kau ṇḍi nyas de'i go 'phang rig ni bzung ba ste
bla ma dam pa de bzhin gshegs pa slob ma rnams kyi ni
gtso bo nyid du chos la yang dag lhag par gshegs pa'o BCt_15.53

sgra de sa la rgyu ba'i gnod sbyin rnams kyis thos nas ni
rnam par rgyas pa'i dbyangs ni rab tu gsol bar gyur pa ste
'byung po rnams kyi 'chi med zhi ba'i ched du nges par ni
dam pa gzigs pas chos kyi 'khor lo bskor ba de legs so BCt_15.54

tshul khrims rtsibs dang zhi dang dul ba'i mu khyud blo rnam yangs
dran pas blo gros brtan pa brtson 'grus lte ba ngo tsha'i gzer
zab pa'i phyir dang rdzun med phyir dang legs par bstan nyid phyir
'jig rten gsum na btsan zhing bstan bcos gzhan rnams kyis mi ldog BCt_15.55

sa 'dzin gnod sbyin rnams las sgra ni nye bar thob byas nas
mkha' la lha yi tshogs rnams kyis ni dbyangs byas shing
de ltar thos nas mtho ris rim dang rim rnams kyis mthon por
tshangs pa'i 'jig rten bar du sgra yis nye bar 'dzegs pa'o BCt_15.56

mtho ris dag na gnas pa'i bdag nyid ldan pa kha cig gis
drang srong che las 'jig rten gsum ni g.yos zhes thos nas ni
sna tshogs yul rnams la ni chags par gshegs pa ma yin zhing
yang dag skye las srid pa gsum na zhi ba nyid du gshegs BCt_15.57

de ltar 'jig rten rnams kyi mchog tu zhi ba'i ched du ni
mtho ris dang ni sa na chos kyi 'khor lo bskor tsam nas
sprin nral mkha' las me tog dang bcas chu yi char bab cing
srid gsum gnas pa rnams kyis rnga bo che rnams mngon par brdungs BCt_15.58

| sangs rgyas kyi spyod pa zhes bya ba'i snyan dngags chen po las | chos kyi 'khor lo bskor ba'i le'u ste bcu lnga pa'o ||

de nas thams cad mkhyen pa yis
rta thul la sogs dge slong rnams
rab snyoms sems ldan de rnams kun
thar pa'i chos la bkod pa'o BCt_16.1

| nyi ma dang ldan skar ma lngas

kun nas bskor ba de mdzes sp BCt_16.2
