byed pa po med 'dir ni rig pa po yang med
bdag po med pa'i lus po 'di ni 'dren par byed
ji ltar 'khor ba'i chu bo rab tu bskor ba ste
smra ba de ni nyon mdzod nyan pa rnams ki mchog BCt_16.90

dbang po drug dang dbang po'i spyod yul drug rnams la
brten nas rnam par shes pa rnam drug 'char ba ste
gsum po so sor reg pa'icho ga rab bskyor zhing
gang las dran dang blo dang las kyis 'jug par yin BCt_16.91

nor bu bud shing nyi ma yang dag phrad pa las
ji ltar me ni sbyar ba'i dbang gis skye ba ste
de bzhin blo dang dbang don dbang po la brten nas
skyes bu la brten bya ba rnams ni thams cad 'gyur BCt_16.92

ji ltar bon las ni myu gu skye ba ste
myu gu des ni sa bon de ni shes min zhing
gzhan las gzhan du ma yin de la de ma yin
de bzhin lus dang dbang po blo yi rim pa'o BCt_16.93

de ltar thub pa mchog gi gzung ni mchog tu dge
dam pa'i don du bsngags pa yang dag thos nas ni
dri ma med pa'i rdul med gzhal du med pa'i
ma ga dha yi bdag po chos mig skyes par gyur BCt_16.94

'khor der ma ga dha yi grong na gnas pa yi
mi ni du ma rnams dang lha na gnas pa rnams
thub pa'i gsung thob pa la rnam dag bsam ldan rnams
'gyur med 'chi ba med pa'i go 'phang thob par gyur BCt_16.95

| sangs rgyas kyi spyod pa zhes bya ba'i snyan dngags chen po las | slob ma mang po dang ldan pa'i le'u ste bcu drug pa'o ||

de nas rgyal po des ni thub la rnam gnas phyir
dpal ldan nags tshal 'od ma'i tshal ni rab phul nas
de nyid khong du chud phyir kun nas gnyis pa ni
mngon par rjes gnang byas pa grong khyer la zhugs so BCt_17.1

de nas gtsug lag khang der 'grol phan pa'i phyir
ye shes las gyur dge ba'i sgron pa bsnams pa ste
tshangs dang lha dang de bzhin 'phags pa rnams kyis ni
gnas pa de dang de yis sangs rgyas rnam par gnas BCt_17.2

de nas rta thul dbang po'i rta ni kun bsdams shing
bsod snyoms 'dod pas rgyal po'i khab ni rab thob ste
gzugs kyis dang ni zhi ba yis dang rnam 'gyur gyis
skye bo chen po rnams kyi mig rnams phrog par gyur BCt_17.3

ser skya'i rigs kyi dge slong slob ma du ma can
sha ra dwa ti'i bu zhes rab tu grags pa yis
dbang po zhi bar 'ongs pa de ni mthong ba ste
lam na rjes su gnas nas tshig ni mngon par smras BCt_17.4

khyod kyi gsar ba'i rtags mtshan dang ni zhi ba nyid
mthong nas kho bo'i blo gros ya mtshan mchog gyur te
de phyir re zhig gal te de nyid rig pa dang
khyod kyi ston pa'i mtshan ci smra ba gang yin smros BCt_17.5

de ltar mchod mang sngon 'gro bram ze de yis ni
de skad brjod cing rta thul gyis kyang smras pa ste
bu ram shing pa'i rigs su rab 'khrung thams cad mkhyen
bdag gi ston pa bla na med pa shes par mdzod BCt_17.6

byis pa gsar bu chos las skyes par gyur pa yis
khyod la ston pa brjod par nus pa ma yin no
smras pa mkhyen pa'i mchog gyur thub pa chen po'i gsungs
nyung ngu cung zad tsam zhig nges par rtogs par mdzod BCt_17.7

gang zhig chos rnams mtshan ma las ni byung ba ste
de dag rnams kyi mtshan ma bcom ldan gyis gsungs shing
gang zhig de dag rnams kyi nges par 'gog pa dang
yang dag 'gog pa de yi thabs gang gsungs pa'o BCt_17.8

de ltar rta thul gyi ni tshig 'di thos nas ni
gnyis skyes nyer rgyal zhes pa'i ming can de yi ni
skyen par chos la mig ni rdul dang bral ba ni
dge zhing rnam par nges par gyur pa'o BCt_17.9

rgyu med pa dang bya ba med dang dbang phyug ste
zhing shes pa ni nges par de yis sngon rig cing
rgyu las 'di rnams rab tu 'jug par thos nas ni
bdag med gyur pa mthong nas dam pa'i bden pa gzigs BCt_17.10

sbom po'i nyon mongs tshogs kyi rnam par nyams pa ni
grangs can lus la cha shas dang bcas mthong ba ste
sbom po dang ni phra mo de yi nyams pa ni
sangs rgyas pa yi bstan las 'gyur zhes snyam par gyur BCt_17.11

bdag tu 'du shes skyes pa nye bar mkhyud nas ni
ngar 'dzin spong ba ma yin de nas nga yi nyid
sgron ma dang ni nyin mor byed pa yod pa na
'od kyi rnam par nyams par gtan tshigs shes bya ci BCt_17.12

ji ltar padma'i chu ba che bar gyur pa yi
snal ma phra mo nyid ni gzhan dang 'brel ba ste
[.. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. ]
[.. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. ] BCt_17.13

[.. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. ]
[.. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. ]
thar pa'i cho ga thar thug min par de snyam zhing
sangs rgyas pa yis rdo ba phye dang mnyam par rtogs BCt_17.14

de nas bram zes rta dul de la mngon mchod nas
tshim zhing rang nyid kyis ni khang par rnam song zhing
bsod snyoms rim bzhin rta thul gyis kyang rab thob nas
rang bzhin gnas shing mkhas pa 'od ma'i tshal du ni BCt_17.15

de bzhin rab tu dad pas mchog dang ldan pa yi
nye rgyal kyang ni mngon du zhugs pa mthong nas ni
thos pa dang ni bsam pas bya ba mnyam pa yi
maudgala rigs su rab tu skyes pas smras pa'o BCt_17.16

dge slong de nyid gang gis gzhan bzhin gyur pa ste
brtan yin yang dag dga' zhing nye bar song
khyod kyis 'chi med ci zhig de ring thob pa ste
bzhin ni rab tu dad 'di gtan tshig med ma yin BCt_17.17

de nas 'di ltar bgyis shes 'di la des bden smras
de nas nges ni bdag la smos pa shes des smras
de nas tshig de nyid ni de yis smras pa ste
thos nas nyid kyi yang dag mig ni skyes par gyur BCt_17.18

las dang bsam pa rnam dag blo ldan de gnyis ni
lag gnas sgron ma bzhin du de nyid mthong ba ste
shes pas ston la rnam par g.yo min bsam ldan dag
de ni blta ba'i don du da lta nyid du gshegs BCt_17.19

slob ma'i sde bcas de nyid rgyang ma nas gzigs nas
bcom ldan drang srong chen pos dge slong rnams la gsungs
shes rab can dang rdzu 'phrul ldan pa rnams kyi gtso
kho bo'i mchog gi slob ma 'di gnyis 'dir 'ongs so BCt_17.20

de nas zab dang brtan pa'i gsung ni zhi ba yi
thub pas de gnyis la ni gtam ngag mdzad pa ste
dge slong 'dir ni mngon par nyer 'ongs rab zhi'i phyir
chos 'di ji lta ba bzhin yang dag thob par gyis BCt_17.21

smyu gu gsum lag gtsug phud dang ldan gnyis skyes de
gnyis la de bzhin gshegs pas 'di skad ces gsungs te
sangs rgyas mthu yis ngur smrig gos dang ldan pa yi
dge slong nyid du skad cig gis ni gyur pa'o BCt_17.22

slob ma'i sder bcas cha lugs de yis de gnyis kyis
mgo bo dag gis thams cad mkhyen la mchod pa ste
de nas sangs rgyas kyis chos de gnyis la gsungs shing
dus kyis de gnyis kyis ni nges legs thob par gyur BCt_17.23

de nas 'od srungs rigs kyi sgron ma gnyis skyes ni
kha dog dang ni gzugs dang nor dang nyer ldan pas
rdzu 'phrul dang ni bdag ldan bzang mo rnam spangs nas
thar pa'i ched du ngur smrig bzung zhing gshegs pa'o BCt_17.24

mdog bzang gser gi mchod rten dang mtshungs 'bar ba ni
bu mang ming bcas mchod rten du ni des mthong nas
dngos po thams cad spangs shing ya mtshan dang bcas pas
thams cad mkhyen la thal mo rab sbyar mngon par song BCt_17.25

thub pa la ni rgyang nas mgo bos phyag 'tshal zhing
phyag 'tshal nas ni ji lta ba bzhin mthon por gsol
bdag ni slob ma bcom ldan bdag gi ston pa lags
mun pa rnams su brtan pa bdag gi sgron mar gyur BCt_17.26

gnyis skyes skom pa skyes shing nye bar 'ongs par ni
mkhyen nas bsam pa rnam dag thar 'dod de la ni
sems la gsung gi chab kyis rab tu tshim mdzad pa
de bzhin gshegs pas legs par 'ongs zhes bka' stsal to BCt_17.27

gsung 'di yis ni ngal ba rnam par sos bzhin te
nges par legs par rtogs pa'i ched du gnas pa ste
de nas dag pa'i bdag nyid 'di la thugs rje can
thub pas chos ni mdor bsdus pa yis gsungs pa'o BCt_17.28

gang phyir thub pas chos ni phra mor gsungs tsam na
de yis don ni mtha' dag yang dag thob gyur te
de phyir yang dag rig dang na tshod che nyid las
dgra bcom 'od srungs chen po nyid du mtshan gyur to BCt_17.29

gang gis lus las gzhan dang yang na lus su ni
bdag dang bdag grib zhes bdag tu rtogs pa ste
de yis bdag tu lta ba de ni nges spangs shing
nyi tshe ba min sdug bsngal 'di ni mthong bar gyur BCt_17.30

tshul khrims brtul zhugs dag gis dag par byed cing gang
rgyu med pa dang rgyu la de yis rtogs pa ste
sdug bsngal nyid dang lam ni yang dag thob nas de
tshul khrims dang ni brtul zhugs mchog tu ma bzung ngo BCt_17.31

phyin ci log tu gyur par song ba gang gi ni
mngon du bskor zhing mchog ni rab tu thob ma yin
bden pa bzhi po'i go 'phang rnams ni mthong gyur nas
the tshom som nyir gyur de yang dag chod par gyur BCt_17.32

'dod pa gang rnams su ni yang dag brgyal nyid dang
brgyal bar gyur dang brgyal bar 'gyur nyid 'jig rten pa
mi gtsang bden pa ma yin de rnams des shes nas
'dod chags shes bya'i yul de spangs par gyur pa'o BCt_17.33

de bzhin du ni byams par gyur pa'i sems kyis des
bshes dang bshes min rnams su khyad par med pa ste
'byung po kun la rjes su brtse ba byas pa yis
nang du song ba'i gnod sems yang thar gyur pa'o BCt_17.34

gzugs la brten rnams dang grong khyer brten pa rnams
sna tshogs nyid dang ldan pa'i 'du shes rnams spangs nas
des ni gzugs kyi khams su chags pa rnams bcom ste
gzugs la 'jug pa'i nyes pa rnams ni rtogs nas so BCt_17.35

rmongs las snyoms 'jug rnams su thar pa'i 'du shes dang
gzugs med lha rnams 'dzad pa can du rtogs nas ni
zhi zhing mtshan ma med pa'i sems ni bzung nas su
gzugs med srid pa la ni chags dang bral bar song BCt_17.36

chu bo sindhu'i shugs chen rab tu 'jug pa bzhin
sems kyi g.yo zhing bskyod par byed pa shes nas ni
brtan pa'i rten las rgod pa rnam par spangs pa ste
zhi zhing rdzing bu gang ba bzhin du gnas par gyur BCt_17.37

snying po med pa'i phyir 'grong ba'i chos nyid phyir
bdag med nyid phyir dngos rnams yang dag rab mthong nas
khyad 'phags nyid dang mnyam dang mchog nyid mthong ba ste
nga rgyal rnam par spangs nas yod ma yin zhes rtogs BCt_17.38

ye shes me yis mi shes mun pa rnam bcom nas
zad pa can dang zad pa med par sna tshogs mthong
rnal 'byor gyis ni rig pa nyid ni yongs bsgoms nas
ma rig pa ni mtha' dag ji lta ba bzhin spangs BCt_17.39

mthong dang bsgom pa dag gis kun tu sbyor ba ni
bcu po 'di dag rnams kyis rnam par grol gyur cing
thal mo sbyar bas sangs rgyas nyid la lta bzhin du
bya ba kun byas rang bzhin gnas te gnas par gyur BCt_17.40

skar ma gsum gyi gnas skabs gsum skyong rjes skyes lha dang ni
ldan pa'i lnga gsum tshes kyi dus su skar ma'i rgyal po bzhin
gsum ni chud zos gyur cing gsum ni lhag par thob pa yi
gsum rig slob ma gsum gyis bde bar gshegs pa rnam par mdzes BCt_17.41

| sangs rgyas kyi spyod pa zhes bya ba'i snyan dngags chen po las | nyan thos chen po rab tu 1a gshegs par mdzad pa'i le'u ste bcu bdun pa'o ||

de nas 'ga' zhig tshe na nor ldan khyim bdag ni
skal ba med pa rnams la nor ni rab sbyin pa
bzang sbyin zhes ni rab tu grgas pa'i min ldan pa
byang phyogs yul ko sa la rnams nas der song gyur BCt_18.1

de yis der ni thub pa bzhugs pa thos pa ste
thos nas blta bar 'dod pas mtshan po rab tu song
rnam dag sems pa des ni rab sleb rab mkhyen nas
rab tu phyag byas pa la bde bar gshegs pas bstan BCt_18.2

gang phyir chos labsgoms pas nyid ni rnam spangs nas
blo ldan mtshan mor bdag la lta 'dod rab sleb ste
da lta nyid du 'ongs pa de yi de ma thag
nges par legs pa'i mgron 'di rab tu long mdzod cig BCt_18.3

gang zhig khyod kyis ltag bsam gang zhig bstan pa dang
bdag gis grags pa nyid las gang zhig dang ba dang
gang zhig sdon gyi rgyu las blo gros rab zhugs te
des ni yon tan chen po rnams kyi snod yin no BCt_18.4

de phyir 'jig rten dag na grags dang gzhan du ni
'bras bu sbyin pa mchog las byung bar rig nas ni
bkur sti byas nas dus su snyoms pa'i bdag nyid kyis
chos las thob pa'i nor ni sbyin par bya ba'o BCt_18.5

tshul khrims yang dag blangs nas spyad par bya ba ste
tshul khrims nyid ni bsrung ba dang ni rgyan yin zhing
'og tu song ba rnams kyi rnam par ldog byed do
nam mkha'i steng gi nges par rdzogs pa po nyid yin BCt_18.6

'dod pa rnams su gcig min zhes pas rjes bcings pa'i
yongs su tshol ba la sogs skyon rnams thos nas ni
nges par 'byung ba'i cho gar yon tan rnam shes nas
rnam dben la skyes shi ba'i bden pa bsnyen par mdzod BCt_18.7

'chi bas nye bar gzir zhing rga bas zil non pa'i
'jig rten rab tu bskor ba yang dag yongs shes nas
zhi ba skye ba med phyir 'bad pa mdzod cig dang
skye ba bden pa med na rga med 'chi ba med BCt_18.8

ji ltar mi rnams la ni mi rtag bdag nyid kyis
rab chags sdug bsngal mngon sum du ni rig mdzod la
de bzhin lha rnams la yang sdug bsngal rig mdzod dang
'jug pa rtag pa nyid ni su yang yod ma yin BCt_18.9

gang du mi rtag pa nyid der ni sdug bsngal zhing
gang du rang nyid med pa der yang sdug bsngal te
gang du bdag ces pa dang bdag gi ba zhes pa
de tshe mi rtag sdug bsngal bdag med gang la yin BCt_18.10

de phyir sdug bsngal las ni sdug bsngal 'di dang ni
mtshan ma las ni 'di yi mtshan ma ltos mdzod la
rnam par nye bar zhi las sdug bsngal zhi ba dang
lam las khyod kyi lam ni dge ba shes par gyis BCt_18.11

'gro ba g.yo ba sdug bsngal 'di ni shes nas su
me dang rab mtshungs dus kyi me yis 'jig rten 'di
mtha' dag rab tu tshig par yongs su rtogs bzhin du
srid dang srid min rnams su smon pa med par gyis BCt_18.12

stong pa nyid dang bdag med bdag gi ba med pa
sgyu ma dang mtshungs 'jig rten 'di ni shes byas nas
'du byed tsam zhig rab tu yongs su rtogs bzhin du
lus 'di la ni khams kyi 'du shes nyid du gyis BCt_18.13

sems ni srid pa g.yos las yang dag g.yos nas dang
'khor ba'i 'gro ba rnam pa sna tshogs mthong nas ni
rtog pa med cing zhi la bden zhing chags med par
sems ni snyoms shing mtshan ma med pa bsnyen par gyis BCt_18.14

de nas drang srong chen po'i chos de thog pa las
chos kyi cho ga'i sngon gyi 'bras bu thob gyur zhing
gang zhig thob nas 'di yi sdug bsngal las lhag ma
rgya mtsho chen po las ni thigs pa gcig bzhin gyur BCt_18.15

chags bral rnams kyi dgon par yang dag gnas kyang ngam
lus med rnam kyis srid rtser yang dag gnas na yang
nags sam lha na de nyid mthong min ma yin la
khyim na gnas pa yin yang lta bas dge legs gyur BCt_18.16

rnam pa sna tshogs lta ba'i dra ba rnams kyis dang
'khor ba'i sdug bsngal rnams kyis de rnams rnam mi 'grol
de phyir rab tu nyams shing de nyid ma mthong bar
chags pa rnam par bsal nas khyad par 'phags pa gshegs BCt_18.17

lta ba legs skyes des ni lta ba ngan de rnams
ston ka'i sprin gyis rdo yi char bzhin spangs pa ste
dbang phyug la sogs mi mthun rgyu las ma yin zhing
des ni 'jig rten rgyu med par min zhes rtogs so BCt_18.18

de phyir mi mnyam rgyur ni 'thad pa ma yin zhing
rgyu med par ni 'gal ba chen po yod pa nyid
'dir yang rigs pa shes pas sos sor mthong ba ste
the tshom med pas de nyid mthong ba kye ma ci BCt_18.19

gal te dbang phyug gis ni 'gro ba skyed gyur na
'gro ba rim gyis rab tu 'jug pa ma yin la
skye dgu rnams kyi 'khor ba'i 'khor lo ma yin zhing
gang du gang zhig bskyed nas de dang de nyid 'gyur BCt_18.20

lus can rnams kyis mi 'dod thob pa ma yin zhing
de yi bdag nyid rnams kyis 'dod pa'i spyod pa med
gang zhig lus can rnams kyi dge dang mi dger gyur
de ni dbang phyug nyid phyir dbang phyug la yin no BCt_18.21

de ni dbang phyug nyid la the tshom 'gyur min zhing
der ni mi rnams dag gis byams pa pha bzhin 'gyur
de la nyam thag pas ni smod pa smra min zhing
lha rnams de dang de la 'jig rten mchod ma yin BCt_18.22

gal te 'di mi bskyed la dgongs par gyur na ni
bya ldan nyid phyir deng 'dir dbang phyug ma yin zing
gal te 'di yis 'jug la 'dod par gyur na ni
de nyid dbang phyug yod pa ny id la byed par 'gyur BCt_18.23

ci ste 'di yi skye la nus pa cung zhig med
byis pa bzhin du 'di yis spyod rnams rgyu med do
gal te dbang phyug gi ni bdag la mda' nyid med
'jig rten bskyed la 'di yi stobs de ci zhig yod BCt_18.24

ji ltar 'dod la gal te bde sdug la bsnen na
'byung po rnams ni 'jig rten na des byas pa nyid
gang phyir 'dod la chags pa khong khrol 'jug ste
de phyir de yi dbang nyid yod pa ma yin no BCt_18.25

de'i rten nyid la sems med rnams kyis gnas bya ste
skyes bu'i 'bad rtsol tshad mar gyur pa nyid yin no
las 'bras med par 'gyur zhing lung ni byas min la
las kyi sbyor ba rnams ni de yi rten yin na BCt_18.26

gal te dbang phyug rang gi las kyis 'gyur na ni
thun mong gyur pa'i las la dbang phyug gyur ma yin
ci ste de yi khyab bdag rgyu med gyur na ni
'gro ba kun gyi dbang phyug nyid ni rab tu grub BCt_18.27

ci ste de yi dbang phyug nyid gzhan las yin zhing
de nyid kyi yang byed po'i dbang phyug gzhan yin la
de yis gzhan zhes de ltar 'dir ni rnam gzhag med
de phyir 'gro ba skyed pa yod pa ma yin nyid BCt_18.28

dbang phyug skyed par gyur na rigs pas tha dad du
rnam par 'gal ba rnam pa du ma mthong ba ste
de yi phyir yang rang bzhin la ni nyes pa de
slar yang rab tu chags par 'gyur ba nyid yin no BCt_18.29

rgyu shes rnams kyi rten ni cung zad rnam log pa'o
rgyu ni bya ba'i cho gar smra ba ma yin zhing
bya ba'i cho gar sa bon la sogs de dang de
ltos pa yin te de phyir rang bzhin rgyu ma yin BCt_18.30

'bras mi rdzogs par byed pa po ni gcig pa nyid
'ga' zhig gi yang rgyu ni cung zad yod ma yin
gcig gi bdag nyid can gyi rang bzhin rab bstan te
de phyir rab tu 'jug la rang bzhin rgyu ma yin BCt_18.31

gang gi rang bzhin gyis ni khyab pa nyid 'dod pa
de yi bya ba med pa nyid kyang rab chags shing
bya ba m agtogs 'bras bu'i cho ga mthong min te
de yi phyir yang bskyed la rang bzhin rgyu ma yin BCt_18.32

de yi khyab pa po nyid la ni rgyu nyid phyir
thams cad las ni thams cad rgyun mi 'chad par 'gyur
'bras bu'i rab tu 'jug la nges pa mthong ba ste
de phyir skyed pa la ni rang bzhin rgyu ma yin BCt_18.33

ji ltar 'di yi yon tan med nyid grub pa ste
de ltar 'bras bu la ni yon tan med nyid 'gyur
rnam 'gyur yon tan can rnams 'jig rten na mthong ste
de phyir rab tu 'jug la rang bzhin rgyu ma yin BCt_18.34

rtag pa'i rgyu las khyad par 'gyur ba ma yin phyir
rnam 'gyur la ni tha dad yon tan nyid ma yin
rnam 'gyur la ni tha dad yon zhugs pa ste
de phyir rang bzhin las ni skyed pa rigs ma yin BCt_18.35

rang bzhin gyis ni bskyed pa'i bdag nyid can nyid la
'bras bu rnams su nyams pa'i rgyu ni grub ma yin
gang phyir rnam 'gyur gyi ni nyams pa mthong ba ste
de phyir rtogs par bya ba rgyu ni gzhan nyid do BCt_18.36

nus par gyur pa'i sbyor la shin tu mthar thug pa'i
thar pa 'dod pa'i sdom brtson rnams kyi ma yin zhing
skye dgu rnams kyi rang bzhin rab tu 'jug pa'i phyir
gang las thar pa'i ched dang pha rol gnon par gyur BCt_18.37

skyed pa'i bdag nyid rang bzhin gyis ni nges nyid phyir
de yi bdag nyid rnam 'gyur la ni nges nyid yin
'jig rten dag na rnam 'gyur la ni brtan nyid med
de phyir rang bzhin gyis ni skyed par rigs ma yin BCt_18.38

sems kyi spyod pa mi gsal rang bzhin zhes bya zhing
rnam 'gyur gsal ba 'di ni de nas grags pa ste
de phyir rab tu 'jug la rang bzhin rgyu min zhing
gsal ba'i rgyu la 'dir ni 'bras bu grub pa nyid BCt_18.39

sems med rang bzhin las ni sems dang bcas pa yi
rta glang bong bu la sogs 'bras bu rigs pa ma yin zhing
sems dang rnam par bral ba'i rgyu rnams dag las ni
sems dang ldan pa cung zad zhig ni 'jug ma yin BCt_18.40

gal te 'gro ba skyed phyir dus ni nges pa ste
de phyir yongs su rtog byed rnams kyis thar pa med
gang phyir skye dgu rnams kyi mtha' ni byas min te
de phyir 'jig rten rgyun chad med par skye bar 'gyur BCt_18.41

gang zhig yon tan rnams kyi gcig dang du mas byas
rjes rnams su ni rang nyid nges pa mthong ba ste
gal te rgyu gcig nyid du gnas par gyur pa na
de yang tha dad khyad par gyur pa ma yin no BCt_18.42

gang zhig smin pa las skyes rdzas kyi cho gar sar
yon tan shes pas yon tan tha dad nyid du mthong
gang phyir rgyu ni khyad par min pa 'dod pa ste
stong pa'i rdzas rnams su yang nges par gyur pa nyid BCt_18.43

gang gi mi gsal ba las rdzas ni 'char ba ste
de yi rjes su dpag pa nges par grub ma yin
'bras bu gsal ba yi ni yang dag rab 'jug pa
mi gsal ba las gang gis mngon du mthong ma yin BCt_18.44

gsal ba gnyis pa dag las rab tu 'jug pa bzhin
mi gsal ba las gang gi 'bras bu dang por gyur
de yi 'dod pa las 'dir mi 'dod chen po'o
rang bzhin nyid kyis nyes pa gnyis ni rab tu chags BCt_18.45

ji ltar gser gyi phreng ba khyad par 'phags pa ste
de ltar rang bzhin gyi ni rnam 'gyur khyad par 'phags
'bras bu khyad par yin zhing rgyu yi ma yin te
de phyir skyed la rang bzhin rigs pa ma yin no BCt_18.46

gal te bya bar skyes bu de ni rgyu yin na
gang gis nges par gang 'dod des de 'thob par 'gyur
'dod kyang kha cig don ni 'thob pa ma yin la
mi 'dod na yang dbang med 'dir ni 'thob par 'gyur BCt_18.47

gang zhig ba glang rta bong rnga mo'i skye gnas 'gro
mnga' bdag nyid du gyur na de ni bsnyen min zhing
de ru 'gro ba'i sdig pa'i las ni byed pa dang
sdug bsngal mi 'dod du yis sdug bsngal byed par 'gyur BCt_18.48

gal te 'jig rten dag na skyes bu byed par gyur
sdug bsngal byed pa ma yin bde ba kho na byed
'dod pa byed par 'dod kyang mi 'dod byed pa ste
dbang phyug chen por 'gyur na mi 'dod su yis spyod BCt_18.49

gang tshe mi ni chos min pa las rnam 'jigs shing
'bad pas chos ni rab tu son par byed pa nyid
sna tshogs nyon mongs rnams kyis dbang med 'phrogs pa ste
de phyir 'di na mi ni pha rol rgyid du gyur BCt_18.50

grang dang dro dang char dang thog dang glog sogs kyi
bya ba rnams ni mi la bzlog nas mthong ba ste
gang phyir rang dbang ma yin mi ni gzhan ldan te
de phyir bya ba rnams su skyes bu dbang phyug min BCt_18.51

gang tshe sa bon las dang sa chu'i rten las ni
dus sbyor rab tu 'jug la lo thog phun tshogs shing
mar me dag las rab gsal shing las me yin te
rgyu med las yin zhes pa rgyu med ma yin no BCt_18.52

rgyu med pa las gal te 'gro ba'i rab 'jug na
mi yi byed pa yis ni med par 'gyur ba ste
thams cad kyis ni thams cad nges par 'thob byed cing
rtag na 'di ni thams cad du ni song bar grub BCt_18.53

bde dang sdug bsngal gal te rgyu med las yin na
gang char kun gyi bde dang sdug bsngal skal min zhing
rgyu med las kyang bde dang sdug bsngal rtogs min te
de phyir rgyu med las shes 'di ni rgyu ma yin BCt_18.54

de skad ces pa la sogs mi mnyam rgyu rnams des
'jig rten rab tu 'jug la rgyu rnams shes ma yin
rgyu med par ni 'jig rten mthong ba ma yin zhing
nyes pa 'di rnams rgyu med las ni yang dag rtogs BCt_18.55

brtan pa dang ni g.yo ba'i 'byung po rnams su yang
de dang de la brten nas de dang de 'byung ste
'jig rten dag na rgyu med ci yang yod min zhing
kun gyi rgyu ni 'jig rten pa yis shes ma yin BCt_18.56

de nas sbyin pa bzang por byin pa'i bzang byin des
rgya che'i chos kyis dam pa'i chos ni rnam shes nas
g.yo ba med pa'i blo gros nges par rab dang bas
drang srong chen po la ni tshig 'di gsal ba'o BCt_18.57

mnyan yod rta ljang rta rid kyis bsnyen grong khyer ni
bdag gi gnas kyi sa ni bsod nams grags pa can
der ni bdag gis khyed kyi gnas ni byed 'dod de
sdig med gnas mchog dam pa de ni bsnyen par mdzod BCt_18.58

gang lta na yang thub pa khyed kyi gnas su snyoms pa ni
gzhal yas khang gi logs sam rnam dben nags su ste
bdag la rjes su brtse phyir gnas kyi ched du ni
dgra bcom rab tu gzhes par mdzad par 'os pa lags BCt_18.59

de nas gtong bar lhag par mos pa 'di yis ni
rnam par grol ba'i sems ni rnam par mkhyen nas ni
chags pa med pa'i blo mnga' blo gros mkhyen pa yis
mchog tu zhi bas blo gros yang dag bka'i stsal to BCt_18.60

sems dpa' brtan kye gang zhig rdzas glog g.yo rnams su
khyod kyis sems dpa' gtong la lhag par mos pa ste
rang bzhin gyis ni sbyin la dga' zhing chos la dgyes
de nyid mthong ba khyed la de ni ngo mtshar min BCt_18.61

gang zhig khyim ni tshig las phyi rol 'thor byed pa
de yi don de 'tshig par byed pa ma yin te
de zin dus kyi me yis 'gro ba tshig pa na
gang gis gang zhig sbyin pa de yis de nyer 'thob BCt_18.62

de phyir rnam spangs sems dpa'i rnams kyis sbyin par dang
yul rnams yang dag longs spyod par ni shes pa nyid
bkren pa 'jig rten dag na zad pa'i skyon mthong bas
nye bar longs spyod ma yin 'jigs las sbyin ma yin BCt_18.63

dus su smod la don ni rnam par gtong ba dang
dpal dang nga rgyal las ni de bzhin g.yul 'gyed par
sems dpa' lhag pa nyid kyis shes te gzhan kyis min
sems dpa' yis ni sbyin pa nyid dang g.yul 'gyed do BCt_18.64

sbyin byed dga' ba nyid du 'gro la 'gro ba ste
snyan pa dang ni dam par grgas pa rab tu 'thob
sbyin pa po yod gang zhes dam pa rnams sbyin nas
yang dag bkur ba dang ni mngon du 'gro bar byed BCt_18.65

de bzhin 'jig rten dag na blo gtang nyid 'gyur zhing
mi bzad pa rnams las kyang nyes pa 'thob ma yin
bsod nams rnams ni bdag gis byas zhes tshim pa ste
'chi ba'i dus su skrag par mdon par 'gro ma yin BCt_18.66

sbyin pa'i 'bras bu 'dir ni me tog tsam zhig ste
sbyin pa po yi 'bras bu gzhan nyid rab tu 'thob
'khor ba'i 'khor lo la ni 'khor ba'i skye bo yi
gtong ba dang mnyam gnyen ni yod pa ma yin no BCt_18.67

mi yi 'jig rten na dang lhan skyes pa rnams
gtong ba las dang mnyam pa rnams las lhag par 'gyur
rta dang glang po'i skye gnas su yang gnas pa rnams
'bras bu de ni gtso bo thob par 'gyur ba'o BCt_18.68

sbyin pas longs spyod rnams kyis yongs su 'dzin pa ste
tshul khrims kyis bsrungs mtho ris su ni 'gro bar 'gyur
ye shes sngon du 'gro ba can gyi zhi ba yis kyang ni
rten dang bral ba gang na grangs su 'gro ba 'gro ma yin BCt_18.69

'chi med bdun rtsi de yis 'thob pa'i ched du yang
sdom par gyur pa rab tu sbyin pa yin pa nyid
sbyin pa dran nas rab tu dga' bar gyur pa ste
yid ni rab tu dga' las nges par ting 'dzin yin BCt_18.70

mnyam par gzhag na yang dag mtho ba 'di ru ni
skye dang 'god pa shes par rim gyis 'gyur ba ste
gzhan la sbyin pa sbyin pa'i sbyin pa po yis ni
snying la gnas pa'i nyon mongs rnams ni bsrabs par 'gyur BCt_18.71

gang zhig sbyin pa byin byed de yi don rnams su
chags par grags pa de ni dang por chod pa nyid
gang la rab tu byams pa'i sems kyis sbyin pa ste
de phyir zhe sdang dang ni nga rgyal spangs par gyur BCt_18.72

rab tu len pa po mi bde ldan rnams mthong nas
gang zhig 'ga' ste des na ser sna yod ma yin
sbyin pa pos ni sbyin pa'i 'bras bu mngon rtogs nas
med pa nyid dang mi shes mun pa 'joms pa po BCt_18.73

de phyir zhi ba 'phags min gyis bsnyen ser sna dang
sred pa ngag las sbyin pa byed pas bcom pa ste
de nas thar pa'i yan lag gyur pa sbyin pa ni
yin zhing nyes pa rab tu thob phyir thar pa'o BCt_18.74

ji ltar gzhan rnams grib ma'i don du shing 'dod cing
kha cig 'bras bu'i don du gzhan rnams me tog phyir
de ltar sbyin pa yongs su sbyin par byed pa ste
kha cig zhi ba'i don du gzhan rnams nor gyi phyir BCt_18.75

de phyir khyad par du ni khyim na gnas rnams kyis
sbyin pa ji ltar nus pa mchog ni gter yin zhing
sbyin pa snying po med pa'i nor gyi snying po ste
dam pa rnams kyi rjes su song ba lam 'di yin BCt_18.76

bza' ba rab tu sbyin par stobs ni rab ster zhing
bgo ba sbyin byed la yang lus ni ster ba'o
gang gis dam pa rnams la gnas ni sbyin byed pa
des kyang 'jig rten dag na thams cad byin pa yin BCt_18.77

theg pa sbyin byed la yang bde ba byin pa ste
mar me sbyin byed la ni spyan mig sbyin pa nyid
de nas dbrog bya ma yin 'chi med rab sbyin zhing
gang gis mthar thug gyur pa'i chos kyis ston pa nyid BCt_18.78

kha cig 'dod pa'i ched du sbyin pa gtong ba ste
gzhan ni don gyi don du gcig ni grags pa'i phyir
kha cig mtho ris don du gzhan ni brtse ba'i phyir
khyod kyi sbyin pa 'di ni chags pa med pa yin BCt_18.79

de phyir legs so khyod ni sred pa de ltar gyur
gang zhig yang dag bsgrubs mdzod 'dod pa tshim par shog
rdul bcas mun pa dang ldan gang khyed 'ongs nas ni
ye shes rnam dag blo ni rab tu 'gro bar 'gyur BCt_18.80

de nyid de bzhin gshegs pas lam gyi yang dag par
dga' ba byas pa dang yang gzhug pa byas pa ni
gtsug lag khang de snying la rnam par byas nas ni
nye rgyal dang ni lhan cig dus su song bar gyur BCt_18.81

song nas de na kau shām rgyal po'i kha ba dang ni
gtsug lag khang gi sa la so sor yang dag rgyas
dpal ldan mnyam zhing mdzes la yid 'ongs shing ldan pa
der ni de yis rgyal byed kyi ni tshal mthong ngo BCt_18.82

de nas de yi don du rgyal byed la zhus te
de yis chags pa las ni de la ma byin no
khyod kyis gal te don gyis kun nas bkram na yang
sa ni bdag gis sbyin pa ma yin zhes smras so BCt_18.83

de nas der ni bzang sbyin gyis de la smras pa
tshal de la ni rin byas shes ni mngon 'dod do
de nas des ni nor gyis sa ni yongs g.yogs nas
chos kyi tha snyad mthong zhing nyod par gyur pa'o BCt_18.84

de yi gtong ba de ni mthong nas rgyal byed gyis
sangs rgyas la ni mchog tu rab tu dang ba byas
nags tshal de yi lhag ma dag ni kun nas ni
de bzhin gshegs pa la ni phul bar gyur pa'o BCt_18.85

de nas mgon med zas sbyin gyis ni drang srong chen po yis
nye rgyal gyis ni nges par gzigs par bya ba'i don ldan par
myur ba'i blo gros dang ldan ma chags grol ba'i sems kyis ni
mdzes shing dge ba mchog gis gstug lag khang ni byed du bcug BCt_18.86

nor gyi dbang phyug nyid kyi gnas ni 'phos pa lta bu dang
byang phyogs ko sha la yi khang pa'i bde ba lta bu dang
de bzhin gshegs pa nyid kyi gzhi ni mtshungs pa lta bu dang
rang gi nor dang stobs kyi dang ni lta ba yi yang ngo BCt_18.87

| sangs rgyas kyi spyod pa zhes bya ba'i snyan dngags chen po las | mgon med zas sbyin la rjes su ston pa'i le'u ste bco brgyad pa'o ||

de nas thub pa sna tshogs tha dad blo can gyi
ston pas thams cad ye shes kyis ni zil mnan nas
bcu phyed phrag ri nas dang grong khyer nas rim gyis
rgyal po bum pas bsnyen pa'i grong khyer du gshegs so BCt_19.1

de nas slob ma stong phrag tsam ni dul ba na
gshegs so des ni yab kyi yul ni rab tu thob
de nas de la rjes su 'dzin pa mdzad bzhed pa
rang gi grong gyi gnas la mtha' ru bsnyen pa'o BCt_19.2

de nas mdun na 'don dang blon po blo gros can
dga' ba'i gtam la dam pa rgyu ba de rnams kyis
yongs su rdzogs pa'i rab brnyes 'phags pa ste
sa skyong rgyal po de la zhus shing gsol ba'o BCt_19.3

de nas de ni 'ongs pa thos nas sa skyong ni
dga' ba yongs ldan sems kyis blta bar 'dod pa yis
grong khyer ba ni kun gyis rjes su 'gro byas pa
myur bas brtan pa spangs shi ng bsu ba la gshegs so BCt_19.4

drang srong dbus su tshangs pa bzhugs pa bzhin du ni
slob mas bskor ba de ni rgyang ring nas gzigs nas
drang srong chen po'i chos la rjes su 'gro bas ni
shing rta spangs nas rkang pa rnams kyis nye bar gshegs BCt_19.5

myur bar de yi nye logs su ni yongs phyin nas
thub pa mthong ba nyid du des ni ma smras so
de la bu zhes smra bar nus pa ma yin zhing
de bzhin dge slong zhes ni nus pa ma yin no BCt_19.6

de nas de yi dge slong cha lugs de mthong zhing
bdag tu song ba'i sna tshogs dpal la brtags nas ni
dbugs ring brgyus nas mchi ma rnam par bton pa de
drag tu mun par gyur cing rnam par zlos pa nyid BCt_19.7

lam 'gro skom par gyur pa mngon par song ba yis
rgyang ring dag nas rdzing bu skam po mthong nas ltar
rang gnas rnam pa dang bral nye bar nyer bzhugs pa
mthong nas bdag gi nyam thag stobs ldan mchog tu gyur BCt_19.8

'jig rten mtha' ru gnas pa'i sems gyur thim pa na
sdig pa'i rnam 'gyur ri mor song ba ji lta bar
gzugs de nyid ni mthong ba na ni bdag la ni
dga' ba yod pa ma yin 'di la dga' ba thal BCt_19.9

gang gis mtha' dag ri yis zlums pas sa gzhi ni
dang po'i dus su nga las nu ni gnas pa bzhin
gang zhig dbang po la yang slong bar 'os min pa
bdag gi de ni pha rol rnams la slong mos 'tsho BCt_19.10

gangs 'di snying po lhun po las ni khyad 'phags shing
gsal bas nyi ma la dang mdzes pas zla ba la
'gros kyis glang po che la dbyangs kyis khyu mchog la
des ni slong mo za zhing sa ni rdzogs la min BCt_19.11

de nas bu yi 'du shes kyis ni 'phyo ba nyid
rgyal po'i bsam pa 'di ni rnam par mkhyen nas dang
'jig rten lhag ma la yang rjes su brtse ba ste
de yi don du sangs rgyas mkha' la 'phur bar gyur BCt_19.12

nyi ma'i shing rta phyag gis reg par mdzad nas ni
rlung gis bsnen pa'i lam la zhabs dag gis gshegs shing
sku la gcig tu gyur zhing du mar gyur pa dang
mang po nyid du gyur nas gcig tu gyur pa'o BCt_19.13

sa la chu bzhin du yang zhugs shing thogs med la
chu yi logs la sa la bzhin du spyod pa dang
ra ba dang ni ri la thad kar mdzad pa dang
thogs pa med cing mkha' la bzhin du rab tu zhugs BCt_19.14

lus kyi phyed kyis chu yi char pa 'bebs pa dang
phyed kyis me bzhin du ni 'bar bar gyur pa ste
ri bos 'bar ba'i sman dang rab tu 'bar ba bzhin
mkha' la gang zhig 'bar dang 'bar bas mdzes par gyur BCt_19.15

dbang phyug mngon par 'dod pa'i skye bo de yi ni
sems kyi rab tu dga' ba de ltar skyed nas ni
nyi ma gnyis pa bzhin du mkha' la bzhugs nas su
mi skyong la ni chos dag bgro bar mdzad pa'o BCt_19.16

mi skyong khyed kyis bdag la gang zhig ltos pa dang
mya ngan rjes su zhugs pa snying rje'i bdag nyid shes
bu la dga' ba de ni chod mdzod zhi bar gshegs
bdag las bu yi 'bras bu gsar pa snoms mdzod cig BCt_19.17

gang zhig sngon chad bu yis pha la ma byin zhing
sngon ni pha yis bu las rab tu ma thob pa
rgyal srid las khyad 'phags shing mtho ris las khyad 'phags
rgyal po mchog gi bdud rtsi de ni bzhes mdzod cig BCt_19.18

sa skyong las kyis bdag nyid las kyi skye gnas dang
las kyi rten dang las kyi rnam smin skal ba dang
las kyi dbang gis gnas par 'gro ba shes nas ni
phan pa'i ched du las gang gyur pa de bsnyen mdzod BCt_19.19

'jig rten de nyid rtogs nas dang ni btsal nas su
dam pa'i las ni mi yi bshes min gzhan ma yin
thams cad bor nas las dang lhan cig khyod kyi ni
rten dang bral zhing gcig pur 'gro bar bya ba'o BCt_19.20

lha'am dmyal ba dud 'gro mi yi 'jig rten du
las kyis rten las son pa'i 'jig rten 'gro ba ste
sred pa'i rgyu ni rnam pa gsum dang skye gnas gsum
sna tshogs las ni 'jig rten pa yis rab tu byed BCt_19.21

de phyir sde tshan gnyis ni yang dag 'jug par yang
lus dang ngag gi las 'di rnam par dag pa dang
yid kyis rab tu zhi la 'bad par bya ba ste
de ni bdag gi don yin gzhan don ma yin no BCt_19.22

'gro ba chu yi dba' rlabs g.yo bar shes nas ni
brtags nas khyod kyis srid pa rnams su dga' mi bya
las ni yongs su zad phyir dam pa'i las gang de
mchog tu bde ba'i don du gang gyur bsnen par bya BCt_19.23

rgyu skar 'khor lo mkha' la bzhin du rtag par ni
'jig rten yongs su 'khor bar shes par byas nas ni
rtse mo 'das nas lha nas lha yang lhung ba ste
kye ma mir gyur smos ci blo gtad byed pa su BCt_19.24

bde ba rnams las mchog tu thar pa'i bde ba dang
dga' ba rnams las bdag tu dga' ba gtsor shes nas
lag 'gro rnams kyis brang la bzhin du bdag ldan ni
su zhig 'jigs pa du ma'i dpal gyis bde la dga' BCt_19.25

de phyir brten pa khyim la mes bzhin 'jig rten ni
'jigs pa chen po dang ni yongs ldan mthong nas ni
gang zhig skye 'chi ngal ba mya ngan dang bral ba
zhi zhing brtan pa'i go 'phang de ni slongs mdzod cig BCt_19.26

don gyis ma yin g.yul gyis ma yin mtshon gyis min
gang la rta dang glang pos don ni yod ma yin
skyon ni dgra bo rnams kyis sde de choms mdzod dang
de las rgyal na rnam par rgyal ba gzhal du med BCt_19.27

sdug bsngal dang ni sdug bsngal gyi rgyu zhi ba dang
zho ba yi yang mngon pa'i thabs ni shes par mdzod
bzhi po 'di yi kur nas khong du chud pa las
'jigs pa chen po dang ni ngan 'gro rnams 'gog go BCt_19.28

de nas bde bar gshegs pas rdzu 'phrul gyi sngon du
zhing du byas pa'i sems la dga' ba skyes pa ste
thos nas mi skyong de yis chos ni rab thob cing
dga' bzhin thal mo sbyar nas 'di skad ces gsol to BCt_19.29

blo ldan dang bcas 'bras bu dang bcas khyed dgyes shing
sdug bsngal chen po las ni rnam grol khyed dgyes so
mya gan ched du don med sa sbyin bdag dga' la
bu yi 'bras bu dang ldan bdag ni dga' bar gyur BCt_19.30

phun tshogs spangs nas gshegs pa khyed ni gnas su gyur
ngal ba chen pos dub las khyed ni gnas su gyur
dga' ba'i gnyen 'dun dga' ba khyod kyis bor ba rnams
bdag cag rnams ni snying rje bar du gnas su gyur BCt_19.31

lha yi drang srong rnams sam rgyal po'i drang srong rnams
de rnams sngon dus na yang gang la ma gshegs pa
nyam thag 'jig rten dag gi dge ba'i ched du lam
nges par legs pa 'di dang khyed kyis lhag par thob BCt_19.32

khyod ni 'khor las sgyur bar gal te gyur na ni
bdag gi dga' ba de ltar 'gyur pa ma yin zhing
rnam pa de ltar rdzu 'phrul 'di dang khyod kyi chos
mthong nas ji ltar bdag gi bstan pa dga' bar 'gyur BCt_19.33

'dir ni yang srid nyid du sbyor ba'i chos la ni
'khor los sgyur bas skye dgu rnams ni skyong ba ste
'khor ba'i sdug bsngal chen po rnams ni 'joms pa la
'jig rten ched du chos kyang thub pa khyod kyis gsungs BCt_19.34

gang gi rdzu 'phrul 'di dang rnam rgyas blo gros dang
'khor ba'i 'jigs pa mtha' dag nges par log pa ni
dpal dang bral yang 'jig rten na khyod dbang phyug ste
dpal ni 'phel yang dbang med sred bcas ma yin no BCt_19.35

brtse ba'i chos kyis bstan pa'i 'os gyur pa
shākya'i rgyal pos mang po de dag smras nas ni
rgyal po nyid dang yab nyid du ni gnas na yang
sras la de nyid khong du chud phyir phyag byas so BCt_19.36

thub pa'i mthu ni lhag par thob pa mthong nas dang
de nyid rab tu 'bigs pa'i bstan bcos mthong nas dang
bla ma rgyal pos sbyar ba'i mchod pa mthong nas ni
du ma rnams kyis rab tu 'byung phyir ro 'dod byas BCt_19.37

de nas gzhon nu mang po 'bras bu la gnas rnams
chos kyi cho ga de nyid rab tu thob gyur te
sngags dang 'dod pa chen po rnams la ltos med nas
byams pa'i gnyen 'dun du ngu ba rnams ni spangs nas so BCt_19.38

kun dga' mdzes dga' kra mi la dang ma 'gags pa
dga' bo nye dga' dag dang de nas 'khyil pa 'dzin
slob ma'i lkog tu ston pa yis ni lha sbyin te
thub pas rjes su bslabs pa de rnams byung bar gyur BCt_19.39

de nas mdun na 'don gyi bu ni bdag nyid che
'char kas lam de nyid la rab tu song ba ste
de yis nges pa rab tu mthong nas de bzhin du
nye ba 'khor dang rgyun shes bu yi blo byas so BCt_19.40

rgyal po yis kyang sras kyi mthu ni mthong nas dang
mchog gi bdun rtsi rgyun ni rab tu thob byas nas
chags pa med par rgyal srid spun zla la byin zhing
rgyal po'i drang srong spyod pas khyim rnams la bsnyen to BCt_19.41

de skad ces pa la sogs legs pa'i gnyen rnams dang
'khor dang gnyen rnams rjes su brtul nas sangs rgyas ni
mchi ma dang bcas grong khyer pa yis mngon dga' ba
rang gnas grong khyer la ni dus su rab zhugs pa BCt_19.42

don kun grub pa zhes pa rgyal po'i sras po ni
don mdzad grub pa grong khyer du ni zhugs pa
zhes ni don thos khang pa rnams su mi mo rnams
sgo rnams dang ni skar khung rnams la mnyam par brten BCt_19.43

mtshams kyi sprin gyis phyed bkag 'od zer ldan pa bzhin
ngur smrig bsnams shing mdzes pa de ni rab mthong nas
bud med de rnams mig nas mchi ma phyung ba ste
padma dang mtshungs thal mo rnams kyis phyag 'tshal lo BCt_19.44

chos kyis dang ni gzugs kyis gsal bar gyur pa ni
'og tu zhal gzigs gshegs pa de ni mthong gyur nas
brtse ba dang ni gus pa rnam par ston pa ste
mchi mas rnyogs pa'i mig can rab myos ma rnams zlos BCt_19.45

legs skyes dbu ni bzhar bar rnam par mdzad nas dang
na bza' rnying pa yongs su gsol nas dang
sku la gzer gyi kha dog rab tu g.yogs nas dang
des ni spyan mig rab tu bkod nas gshegs | BCt_19.46

gang zhig gdung ba skyob pa'i gdugs dkar bsnyen phyir dang
sras po rnam par ngul ba blta ba'i phyir 'ongs shing
kun nas gnas phyir 'os shing rgyal ba'i phyir 'os pa
des ni lhung bzed yang dag yongs su bzung nas gshegs BCt_19.47

'gram par ta ma la yi lo ma rnam bkod pa'i
mdzes ma'i gdong dang gdung ba skyob pa'i gdugs dkar ni
gang gis bsnyen par 'os shing mgyogs 'gro 'os pa ste
des ni lhung bzed yongs su bzung nas rkang pas gshegs BCt_19.48

sa skyong bdag skyes rnams kyi dgra rnams zad par dang
dga' ba rnams kyi chags dang 'gro ba'i rjes chags par
blta bar 'os shing sna tshogs dbu rgyan bsnams pa gang
des ni sa yi gnya' song gang tsam gzigs shing gshegs BCt_19.49

'di yi blta ba ci zhig mtshan nyid de ni ci
don gnyer ci zhig rol pas dgra bor gyur pa ci
gang 'di brtul zhugs dang ni lhan cig rol ba ste
bu yis rnams dang mo mtsun mdzangs ma rnams dang ni BCt_19.50

rgyal po'i mna' ma nges par mya ngan 'dzin ma'o
grags 'dzin ma de shin tu dka' thub byed pa ste
gang gis jo bo'i rab tu spyod pa 'di thos shing
thos nas kyang ni gnas shing nyams par 'gro ba med BCt_19.51

'di yi gzugs ni nges par rjes su mthun pa dang
kha dog ngan pa'i gzugs 'di snang ba mthong nas ni
sras 'dod mi dbang rgyal po ji lta bur gyur zhing
'tshe ba'i dgra bo la yang ji lta bur byed dam BCt_19.52

mchi mas gang ba'i sras po sgra gcan 'dzin mthong nas
gal te de lta nyid du 'di ni chags ma yin
byams pa'i gnyen rnams las kyang gzhan du kha bltas pa
'di 'dra nges pa'i brtul zhugs la ni dge legs shog BCt_19.53

gzi mdongs dang ni lus kyi dbyibs dang 'gros sam ste
bda ba'i rab tu 'jug la nges par tshad ma yin
yon tan de rnams dag gis 'di ni mdzes pa ste
zhi bas ldan zhing yul rnams kyis ni rnam par bral BCt_19.54

sna tshogs ston ni rang mtshungs bsam pa yang dag yongs bzung nas
de skad ces sogs rab myos ma rnams mang po rnam par labs
sangs rgyas ma chags thugs kyang rang gi grong khyer la gshegs nas
bsod snyoms brnyes shing nya gro dha yi mtshan ma'i nags su gshegs BCt_19.55

nyung ngu nyung ngu'i bsod snyoms sbyin pa rnams kyis nor rdzas phra zhing dge ba ma byas skye bo sgrol bar mdzad bzhed pa
spyod pa 'di yis yang dag tshim pa ma yin dge sbyong skye bo bsam pa mthu la ba la brten par mdzad bzhed la
'jig rten dag na skyid de ba zhes rgol ba nub par mdzad bzhed de bzhin yongs su bris nyid ston par mdzad bzhed pa
brtag par snyam la bsod snyoms phyir ni yab kyi grong khyer la ni sred med thugs mnga' de bzhin gshegs pa zhugs par gyur BCt_19.56

| sangs rgyas kyi spyod pa zhes bya ba'i snyan dngags chen po las | yab dang sras mjal ba'i le'u ste bcu dgu ba'o ||

| skye bo chen po'i rjes su brtse ba mdzad nas ni
bde bar 'pham byed kyis ni phyag gis mngon bsrungs pa'i
grong khyer la ni chen po'i tshogs kyis rab tu dpags
[.. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. ] BCt_20.1

me tog rab rgyas mya ngan med pas gsal byas shing
yan lag dmar por gyur cing khu byug skad sgrogs pa
ti se'i gangs ltar mtho ba'i lding khang phreng ba can
dpal ldan rgyal byed tshal ni de nas rab tu thob BCt_20.2

des ni gtsang ma'i chus gang phreng ba dkar po can
gser gyi bum pa dang bcas bum pa blangs nas ni
de nas dus su rgyal byed tshal ni bzang sbyin gyis
de bzhin gshegs pa la ni rab tu phul bar gyur BCt_20.3

de nas shā kya thub pa lta 'dod rgyal po ni
de ltar 'pham byed rgyal byed tshal du song ba ste
song nas de nas bkur sti byas te thub pa la
rab tu btud cing gdan byas tshig 'di gsol ba'o BCt_20.4

thub pa grong khyer 'dir ni khyed kyi gnas bzhed pa
nges par rang ni ko sa la rnams kyi dge ba'o
de nyid gzigs pa 'di 'dra brten pa med pa ni
nye bar 'tshe byas yul ni skal ba med pa'am BCt_20.5

khyed mthong ba 'am yang na mngon par phyag 'tshal ba
yang dag thob po bdag cag rnams kyi rjes bzung phyir
dam pa rnams kyi 'dus pa thob nas 'jig rten na
tshim pa med kyang ji ltar tshim pa nyid yin no BCt_20.6

gang gis rten can rlung ni rab tu g.yos pa ste
de yi bdag nyid las ni nye ba las 'gro ste
mkha' 'gro'i bya rnams lhun po'i 'dus pa nyer thob nas
tab bzhin rnam par spangs nas gser du 'gyur ba'o BCt_20.7

de phyir 'di dang che ge mor ni mgon gyur zhing
skye bo legs pa'i rten las gzhan min bdag gi nags
ga dha'i sras po thub pa chen po rab thob nas
phur bu gsum pa'i khyim ltar lha na mdzes par gyur BCt_20.8

'jig rten dag na rnyed pa rab rnyed sna tshogs pa
tshad dang lhan pa dag ni mdzad pa can yin la
khyod kyi nye ba las ni don gang yin pa rnams
de dag rnams kyi grangs med nyams pa yod ma yin BCt_20.9

legs pa khyod kyi nges pa'i lta ba'i lta ba las
'di las gzhan du rnyed pa shes pa ma yin zhing
khyab bdag bdag ni gnod pa rnyed bla sdug bsngal ba
chags pa dang ldan rgyal po'i chos la spyod par 'gyur BCt_20.10

de ltar dbang po dang mtshugs rgyal po de yis ni
rnam pa de ltar mngon du gyur te gsan nas ni
don dang 'dod pa dag ni chags pa mkhyen nas su
de yi bsam pa yang dag bskul ba thub nas gsungs BCt_20.11

mi dbang khyod kyi tshig 'di ngo mtshar che ma yin
khyod kyi spyod pa 'di ni legs pa rnams la min
'og nas 'phos pa 'gro bar 'dod pa rnams kyis ni
phan pa 'dod pa'i dam pa'i skyes bu rnams la sdang BCt_20.12/13

gang phyir sa skyong khyed kyi dgongs pa de nyid ni
des na khyod la 'dir ni cung zad smra 'dod de
de ni shes par gyis shig bdag gi lta ba ni
'bras bcas ji ltar gyur pa khyed kyi de ltar gyis BCt_20.14

mi skyong rgyal po'i dus kyis bcings nas bkug pa na
mdza' bshes ma yin gnyen min phun tshogs rjes 'gro min
thams cad kyis ni dman zhing dbang med 'gro ba ni
grib ma bzhin du las gcig rjes su 'gro ba nyid BCt_20.15

de phyir mtho ris dang ni grags pa dam pa ni
mngon par 'dod bzhin chos kyi rgyal srid rjes su skyongs
rmongs pa las ni chos 'khrul ba'i rgyal po yi
rgyal srid de nyid mtho ris na yang ma yin no BCt_20.16

'dir ni rgyal srid yang dag yongs su bskyangs nas ni
chos las ring min rta rid mtho ris rab 'thob nas
'dir ni rmongs las myi yi bdag po ni ku mbha
chos las 'phos shing ka shi rnams su la zhugs BCt_20.17

'phags pa yi dang sdig pa yi ni las kyi ni
khyod la dper bstan shi ba bdag gis de smras te
rang gi skye dgu rnams ni rtag tu legs bsrungs shing
dpyad nas de phyir brtan pa dge la 'bad pa gyis BCt_20.18

ji ltar srog chags rnams ni gtse bar ma byed cig
rtag par dbang po rnams ni rol bar ma byed cig
'phags min gyis bsnyen khro ba 'dzin par ma byed cig
phyogs min bya bar sems ni g.yo bar ma byed cig BCt_20.19

nga rgyal nyid kyis skye bo dam pa ma smad cig
bshes gnyen 'du shes dka' thub rnams ni ma 'joms shig
nyon rmongs dbang gis dam pa'i brtul zhugs ma byed cig
dam pa min pa'i lta ba cung zad ma bsnyen cig BCt_20.20

mtshar la ma 'gro mi dge'i lam la ma gnas shig
rgyags par ma 'gro dga' min mi bzod ma nyam cig
snyan grags mi bzang brdzun la blo gros ma 'dzin cig
bstan bcos mthong las lhag par gtor ma ma 'phrog cig BCt_20.21

blo ni mnyam par shog cing chos ni gyis mdzod cig
dam pa rnams dang sbrel mdzod ri mo khod mdzod cig
ji ltar phul byung 'di ni thob nas slar yang ni
rgya cher mngon par 'gro ba de ltar gyis mdzod cig BCt_20.22

brtson 'grus brtsams nas dang ni bstan pa yongs bzung nas
rigs pa rnams ni bskyed nas skyon rnams zil mnan nas
'chi ba yang dag dran nas 'phags pa'i bya ba gyis
che ba'i bdag nyid thob nas zhi lam thob par gyis BCt_20.23

gang gi 'bras bu 'di ni zhi ba skyong ba ni
las de nyid ni slar yang byed par 'os pa ste
yid gzhungs ldan pa 'di dang byed pa byas pa nyid
'bras bu gang zhig mthong bas sa bon bskrun par byed BCt_20.24

'di na mchog gyur gang zhig sdig pa byed pa ste
snang ba de ni mun par gnas pa bdag gi lugs
chos ni gtso bo skyes bu gtso bo ma yin pa
mun pa snang ba la ni gnas pa bdag gi lugs BCt_20.25

khyad 'phags gang zhig chos kyi cho gar 'jug pa ste
dkar po dkar por mchog tu 'gro ba bdag gi lugs
dman pa gang zhig sdig pa'i las ni byed pa ste
de yang mun pa mun pa'i mtha' ru 'gro ba lugs BCt_20.26

de phyir phung po bzhi po de rnams shes byas nas
rgyal po 'bad pa gyis shig de ltar ji ltar 'dir
bde nas bad par gal te 'gro bar 'dod na ni
phyogs ni gsum par bsnyen zhing snga ma yin no BCt_20.27

gzhan gyis gzhan la dge ba byed pa ma yin zhing
ci ste byed na de la rjes su 'gro ma yin
byis pa'i nyams pa yod min rang la 'thob pa ste
ma byas pa yi 'ong ba 'grub pa yod ma yin BCt_20.28

ma byas pa yang brgya la byed pa ma yin zhing
ma byas pa ni gzhan du dge legs 'gyur ma yin
der ni 'gro ba la yang nor ni yod min te
de phyir dge ba'i las kyi cho gar 'bad pa bgyis BCt_20.29

gang zhig sdig pa lhag par spyod pa legs min zhing
gson pa'i 'jig rten na de'i bdag la dga' ma yin
bdag gi ched du bdag gis sdig pa byas nas ni
gzhan du 'bras bu bdag nyid kho nas longs spyod do BCt_20.30

rgyal po chen po ri bo chen po bzhi rnams ni
'ongs pa rnams su 'gro ba kun nas srub pa ste
chos kyi bya ba rnams pa sna tshogs bsten las ni
ji ltar 'thad pas gzhan na bya ba ci zhig yod BCt_20.31

rga dang rgud pa nad dang de nas 'chi ba ste
bzhi po 'di rnams de bzhin du ni ongs pa ste
ri bro rnams kyis kun nas bskor ba bzhin du ni
'jig rten mtha' dag dbang med 'khol bar byed pa'o BCt_20.32

de nas 'ongs pa rnams su dbang med sdug pa bsngal te
rten ni yod min mngon du 'thab min srung ba med
der ni byed pa'i ched du nor med chad pa med
chos las ma gtogs sman gzhan yod min na BCt_20.33

de ltar mi rtag gyur na gson pa'i 'jig rten na
glog ni g.yo ba'i yul la rab tu zhugs pa na
'chi ba'i lag pa'i rtse la yongs su gnas pa ste
chos ma yin pas 'bras bu 'ongs spyod par 'os min BCt_20.34

dbang chen dang mtshungs mi dbang de dang de rnams ni
g.yul du lha yi mngon par 'thab la phyir nas kyang
rab tu rgyas pa rnams dang nges par zum pa rnams
dus kyi dus su bde dang sdug bsngal skal ba'o BCt_20.35

'byung po 'dzin pa'i sa yang zad par 'gro ba ste
'jig pa'i mes ni lhun po de bzhin sreg par byed
rgya mtsho chen po yongs su bskams par 'gro ba ste
dbu ba dang mtshungs mi yi 'jig rten kye ma ci BCt_20.36

shugs byas nas kyang rlung ni zhi bar 'gro ba ste
'jig rten gdungs nas kyang ni nyi ma nub par 'gro
bsregs nas kyang ni me nyid 'da' bar nyer 'gro ste
gang de de ltar gnas par 'gyur ba yin snyam mam BCt_20.37

lus po 'di ni yun rings dus su bsrungs kyang ngam
sna tshogs longs spyod rnams kyis nye bar bskyangs kyang ni
de yis 'dir ni nyin zhag 'ga' zhig bzhugs nas su
[.. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. ] BCt_20.38

nga rgyal dang ni rgyags pa khur nas dus su ni
rab tu 'thor zhing shin tu gyur pa gnyid log gyur
rnam pa de ltar 'jig rten 'gro ba shes nas su
de la ma nyal dge ba la ni gnyid ma log BCt_20.39

'khor ba'i phyogs ni g.yo bar 'dzegs nas su
nges par lhung nas gzhi bag med 'gyur ba'o
[.. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. ]
[.. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. ] BCt_20.40

gang zhig bda ba 'brel min de ni bsnyen bya min
gang gis 'bras bu legs min gang de bya ba min
gang zhig dge la sbyor min de ni bshes ma yin
sdug bsngal rnam par 'joms min gang de ye shes min BCt_20.41

gal te ye shes min na yang srid ma yin zhing
srid par gyur na lus med nyid la yin pa ste
lus su gyur na yul las thar pa ma yin zhing
nyi tshe ma yin 'dod pa'i srid pa don med do BCt_20.42

gang phyir lha na gnas rnams dus kyi dbang gis ni
gzugs med rnams kyang mdzad pa can phyir mi rtag ste
de bzhin 'jug pa min la blo gros zhugs bya zhing
gal te 'jug pa med na sdug bsngal yod ma yin BCt_20.43

gang phyir lus ni 'gro dang gnas pa la sogs pa'i
sna tshogs rten gyi sdug bsngal dag gi rtsa ba ste
de phyir lus med du ni ye shes nus pa gang
de yod lus kyi bu lon yod pa ma yin no BCt_20.44

gang las 'gro bas 'dod pa'i ched du bskyed pa yis
sdug bsngal chen po dum rnams la nyer 'gro ste
'di las 'dod pa'i srid las rnam par dben nus shing
sdug bsngal rnams las chags med nyam thag yod ma yin BCt_20.45

de phyir gzugs dang bral ba'i lha rnams na yang ngam
'dod pa rnams dang ldan pa'i gzugs ldan rnams na yang
skor ba nyid phyir gzugs pa zhi ba ma yin na
'dod pa spyod pa drug po rnams su sngon nyid do BCt_20.46

rnam pa de ltar mi rtag sdug bsngal de med cing
rtag par 'bar ba'i 'jig rten gsum po nyid mthong nas
bya tshang shing la sgong skyes rnams kyis gdung ba ltar
gang du 'jug la smon lam rigs pa ma yin no BCt_20.47

mchog de rig par bya zhing gzan ni rig bya min
mchog de blo gros yin zhing gzhan ni blo gros min
mchog de bya ba yin zhing gzhan ni grub pa min
[.. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. ] BCt_20.48

chos 'di khyim dang ldan pa'i skye bo rnams kyis te
yod pa min zhes de ltar nges par rig bya min
nags sam khyim na gnas pa dag gi zhi ba ni
gang gis sgrub pa yod pa de yis yod pa'o BCt_20.49

tshad pas mngon par gdungs pa chu la rnam zhugs te
spyi las thams cad tshim pa nye bar 'gro ba nyid
sgron ma dang ldan mun pa ru ni mthong ba ste
rnal 'byor tshad ma'o na tshod ma yin rigs ma yin BCt_20.50

kha cig nags na gnas kyang na tshod la mi sbyor
brtul zhugs zad cing ngan 'gro la ni bsnyen pa nyid
kha cig khyim na gnas kyang rnam dag las can ni
bag dang ldan pa nges legs la ni bsnyen pa'o BCt_20.51

mun pa'i rgya mtsho la ni lta ngan dba' rlabs can
sred pa'i chu la srog chags rnam par 'phyo rnams su
shes rab gru bo dran dang brtson 'grus skya ba ni
gang gis yod pa de ni de la sgrol ba yod BCt_20.52

de ltar yul la mchog tu song ba'i rgyal po de yis ni
thams cad mkhyen las chos kyi de nyid 'di ni nyer thob nas
rgyal srid ngan pa mi rtag g.yo zhes nyer skyes blo can ni
myos pa dang bral gnyis 'thung bzhin du mnyan yod nyid du zhugs BCt_20.53

sa dbang btud pa de ni shes nas mu stegs can gzhan rnams
der ni stobs bcu ba la rdzu 'phrul gyis ni 'gran btsugs gyur
sa skyong las ni rnam par gsol nas de nas bdag 'pham pa'i
drang srong gis ni rdzu 'phrul ched du sdug pas gnas pa byas BCt_20.54

de nas gsal zhing 'od zer 'phro ba dang bcas dkyil 'khor can
skar ma rnams ni 'bar bar gyur pa'i nyi ma shar ba bzhin
yang dag dga' zhing rnam pa sna tshogs blo can ston pa rnams
der ni thub pas rdzu 'phrul rnam pa mang pos pham par mdzad BCt_20.55

de nas mnyam yod kyis ni de las skyes pa'i grags pa dang
bkur sti nges pa mchog gi dpal gyis yongs su spangs par gyur
de nyid kyis ni srid pa gsum las gyen du 'dzegs pa ste
de'i phyir chos dag gsung bar bzhed cing yul la phan phyir ro BCt_20.56

de nas thub pa mtho ris gnas pa'i yul ni ye shes kyis
rnam par btul nas mtho ris gshegs pa lo ni rnam phul des
mkha' la lha yi rgyal po'i bsod snyoms cho ga bzhin bzhes nas
lha yi 'jig rten dag nas sām ka par ni yang dag babs BCt_20.57

de la gzhal med gnam sa'i logs la babs pa yi
zhi ba thob cing ltos pa dang bcas lha rnams rjes su 'ongs
sar gnas nam mkha'i logs la gyen du gdong phyogs rgyal po ni
de dang de rnams mgo bo rnams kyis btud cing rab tu bzung BCt_20.58

| sangs rgyas kyi spyod pa zhes bya ba'i snyan dngags chen po las | rgyal byed kyi tshal rab tu bzhes pa'i le'u ste nyi shu pa'o ||

thar 'dod lha na gnas rnams dang
skyed ma mtho ris su btul nas
thub pas gdul bya rnams 'dul zhing
de nas de ni 'jig rten rgyus BCt_21.1

ri lnga'i dbus kyi grong khyer du
'od ldan 'tsho byed dbang po dang
gro bzhin skyes dang yan lag sbyin
rnam par 'dren pas de nas btul BCt_21.2

rgyal po'i bu ni 'jigs med dang
dpal sbas dang ni nye bar 'khor
nya gro dha sogs mthar ldan rnams
snga ma'i lta ba las bzlog go BCt_21.3

chos kyi thos pa nyid las ni
mi skyong dpal ni yangs pa can
spos 'dzin gyi ni dbang phyug 'dir
pa-dma zhes bya rnam par btul BCt_21.4

de nas gnod sbyin gangs ldan dang
rtse mo brgya pa de nas ni
rnam rgyas pha rol gnon pa yis
rnam rgyas ri bor btul ba'o BCt_21.5

yon tan gzigs pas mi skyong ni
lta byed btsun mo'i 'khor bcas la
'tsho byed a mra'i nags tshal du
mtshan mo dad pas sbyar bar mdzad BCt_21.6

de nas pha rol 'gro ba can
bram ze zhi bar 'gro rnams des
rdo ba'i ri bor phra mo yi
tshigs bcad don rnams klog tu bcug BCt_21.7

de nas dam pa dran mdzad pas
dngos su nor sbyin mthong ba mo
dga' ba'i skyed ma legs ldan ma
'od ma'i tsher ma can du btul BCt_21.8

de nas brtan ldan grong khyer du
brtsegs sbyin gnyis skyes dam pa ni
mchod sbyin rnam pa sna tshogs kyis
mchod 'dod thar pa'i chos la btsud BCt_21.9

de nas lus 'phags ri bo ru
bcubcud phyed rtse mo nyid dang ni
lha min skyes ma dang lha rnams
nges par 'dzin du btsud par gyur BCt_21.10

de nas a ngga'i grong khyer du
gnod sbyin gang ba bzad po dang
mchog dang dbyug pa dkar dmar dang
gtum po lto 'phye che rnams btul BCt_21.11

a pa ṇa yi grong khyer du
bram ze ke bya she la dag
[.. .. .. .. .. .. .. ]
dka' thub thob pa thar par sbyar BCt_21.12

'tshe byed sor mo'i phreng ba can
bran bzangs dang mtshungs gnyis skyes ni
bcom ldan rdzu 'phrul phun tshogs kyis
phra mo rnams su btul bar mdzad BCt_21.13

gang ba bzang po dang mtshungs rdzas
lug ces bya ba bzang pos 'tsho
nor sbyin bzang dang bzang po'i bu
bzang por yang dag rtogs par mdzad BCt_21.14

de nas tshangs pa'i tshe ldan ming
rnam rgyas tshangs pa'i tshe ldan pa
gang gi smra ba smra mchog gis
lus 'phags po yi grong du pham BCt_21.15

yangs pa can gyi rdzing bu ru
srin bu sha za dang seng ge
la sogs li tstsha bī rnams dang
mchog dang bden byed nyid btul to BCt_21.16

de nas las bzang pos gnod sbyin
bzang po bzang po'i sems ldan pa
rgyan byed dang mtshungs grong khyer du
chos kyi lam la btsud pa'o BCt_21.17

de nas blo dang ldan pa yis
shin tu mi bzang 'brog tu ni
gnod sbyin 'brog gnas zhes bya dang
gzhon nu legs 'ongs la stog to BCt_21.18

de nas gnod sbyin sdig med la
gnod sbyin bdag pos phyag byas pas
bde dga'i grong du thar pa ni
thar pa gzigs pas gdams pa mdzad BCt_21.19

thub pa grags pa yangs rnams dang
gnod sbyin drag po'i lam can dang
kha spu ldan pa gnyis la ni
ga yar drang srong gis bstan to BCt_21.20

de nas drang srong dkar min gyi
tsha bo kā tyā ya na ni
bā rā ṇa si'i grong du sngon
gnyis skyes stobs bcu ldan pas btul BCt_21.21

mtsho 'obs bde bar pha rol 'gro'i
grong la rdzu 'phrul gyis gshegs nas
dus su tshangs pa rna bstod la
de nas des ni rjes su bstan BCt_21.22

rjes su bstan de rab dad pas
drang srong mchog gi gtsug lag khang
rtag par dri ldan kha la reg
tsa-nda na rang bzhin byed du bcug BCt_21.23

de nas gang du thub pa'i zhabs
rdo las 'khor lo'i mtshan mthong bas
ser skya dka' thub ldan pa ni
'od zer ldan pa des btul lo BCt_21.24

de nas gnod sbyin glang po la
glang po ldan par bstan pa ste
de bzhin drag po bong bu ni
bcom brlag tu ni btul ba'o BCt_21.25

yul 'khor skyong dang rdzas mnyam pa
yul 'khor skyong zhes dran pa ni
grong rdal rags pa'i mdzod ldan du
ston pas de nas rnam par btul BCt_21.26

tshangs pa dang 'dra skye bo mchog
dgra can du ni btul ba ste
mkhas pa rgya chen skyes bu can
nyon mongs dul bar de bzhin no BCt_21.27

'jigs bcas kyi dang mtshams bzangs kyi
bu'i bu mos 'jug bu dag dang
mu stegs gzhan rnams kyi mun pa
mnyan yod nyid du thub pas bcom BCt_21.28

'dir ni bram ze mchod sbyin can
dge sogs rnams dang rigs gtsang dang
ko sa la yi dbang phyug ni
sangs rgyas nyid kyis dad pas sbyar BCt_21.29

de nas bram ze mkhas pa ni
bram ze su ka sā ri dang
she ta bi ka'i 'grog zhi bar
bstan pa mchog gis bstan pa'o BCt_21.30

de nas 'thob pa'i grong khyer du
grong khyer gtso dang dus byed dang
'jigs pa'i las can chu srin klu
rab tu ma zhi zhi bar mdzad BCt_21.31

de nas bhar ga rnams su des
gnod sbyin 'jigs byed btul mdzad cing
rigs med kyi ni bla ma gnyis
rgan po de bzhin rjes su bzung BCt_21.32

nor ldan gyi mchog dbyangs ldan dang
bud med sgur mchog sogs rnams dang
skyes chen de rnams de rnams ni
kau shām bīr ni rjes su bzung BCt_21.33

de nas spos 'dzin yul nyid dang

nang gi pha rol son par gshegs BCt_21.34

dus su de nas gdams ngag bstan BCt_21.35

de la sogs pa'i 'byung po rnams

sangs rgyas grags pa 'phel bar gyur BCt_21.36

'dra ba min pa mang po byas BCt_21.37

nye bar bcom pa'i sems ldan des
thub pa dge 'dun dben byas shing
'phye las 'dod pa ma byas te
de la gnod pa'i phyir btsams so BCt_21.38

de nas bya rgod phung po'i rir

thub pa'i sting du gang 'phangs pa
lhung ba ma yin gnyis su gyur BCt_21.39

'jig rten dus su chu 'dzin sngon po sgra sgrogs pa

de bzhin gshegs pa la ni mngon du gdong phyogs par
glang po'i dbang po rgyal po'i lam la gtad pa'o BCt_21.40

lus kyis snun pas yan lag mchog ni nyer blangs shing
| mche bas phug pas rgyu ma'i dra ba rab bkram pa'i
lus po rnams kyis rgyal po'i khab kyi lam rnams ni
rgyu bar dka' bar byed la mngon par rab tu zhugs BCt_21.41

sha ni 'dod pas mi yi brla la rmugs pa ste
mche ba'i rtse mos reg cing g.yo ba'i rgyu ma'i phreng
khrags gis gsher ba'i mgo bo sna ljags drag po yis
'phen pa'i don du rdo rnams bzhin du gyen du 'phen BCt_21.42

gsum du rab dga'i chang gis 'thor ma'i dri ldan zhing
rul pa'i khrag dang zhag gi dri yis bsgos rnams kyis
de tshe bskor zhing mtha' med khro ba dang ldan pa
grong khyer skye bo de la skye bas 'jigs par byed BCt_21.43

gnyis 'thung myos pa dus kyi dbyug pa 'jigs 'dra ba
khengs las gdong ni bcos shing sgra skad 'thon pa ste
khros pas rnam par log pa'i mig can de mthong nas
hā hā byed pa rgyal po'i khab nas byung bar gyur BCt_21.44

kha cig yid mi bde bas phyogs su bros pa ste
gzhan ni mtho ba min pa'i yul rnams la thim zhing
de bzhin 'jigs pa las gzhan 'jigs pa ma bzung nas
gzhan rnams gzhan rnams dag gi khyim rnams la zhugs so BCt_21.45

kha cig rnam par 'dug pa'i seng ge'i sgra rnams ni
rang gi srog la the tshom yang dag ma bsams shing
sangs rgyas la ni mngon par 'tshe ba ma byed ces
rab tu bzung nas gnyis 'thung de la rgyab nas 'bod BCt_21.46

de bzhin gzhan rnams glang po skyong la 'bod pa ste

de nas de la gzhan rnams bsdigs par byed pa ste

rlung 'gro skar khung dag nas rnam par lta bzhin du

de la dbang po'i glang po ches kyang reg pa ru
nus pa ma yin gang phyir thub pa brtan par gshegs BCt_21.50

gang phyir sangs rgyas la ni rjes 'gro dge slong ste

sna tshogs bdag nyid 'jig rten rang bzhin gyis bzhin du
kun dga' bo gcig sangs rgyas la ni rjes su song BCt_21.51

de nas glang chen khros pa de ni nyer 'ongs nas

mig sman ri bo rdo rjes phye mar bcom pa bzhin

de la shin tu mdzes shing 'dam skyes 'jam po yis
legs skyes sor mo'i dra ba'i phyag gis mgo bo la
zla ba chu 'dzin la ni 'od zer gyis bzhin du
gnyis 'thung dbang po la ni thub pas reg par gyur BCt_21.53

chu yi shin tu khur las dus kyi sprin bzhin du

de la sems can ma 'os zhi bas bstan pa'o BCt_21.54

sdig med dang bcas rnam par 'joms pa sdug bsngal te

srid pa srid par sdig med bcom pa'i srog chags kyis
bde 'gro brgyad la glang chen 'gyur ba ma yin no BCt_21.55

'dod chags dang ni zhe sdang de bzhin gti mug ste

chang gsum rnams dang thub pa rnams ni bral ba ste
rims nad med cing mya ngan 'das pa mngon par brnyes BCt_21.56

de phyir mun par 'dod pa 'di ni spongs 'dod pa

'khor ba'i rgya mtsho'i 'dam ni rgyas par chags pa ste
slar yang de ltar gnyis 'thung dbang po ma ltung cig BCt_21.57

de nas glang po des ni gsung 'di thos nas su
chang ni spangs shing yang dag rig par song ba ste

nang du song ba'i bde ba dam pa thob par gyur BCt_21.58

gzhan rnams 'phags pa nyid las glang chen la bstod cing
ya mtshan dang bcas gzhan rnams reg par gyur pa'o BCt_21.60

lding khang la gnas bud med gzhan rnams de la ni
gtsang zhing rin thang chen po'i gos rnams kyis mchod cing

rgyan ni de dang de dag rnams kyis mngon par 'thor BCt_21.61

dus dang mtshungs pa'i glang po dul bar gnas pa na

dad pa la gnas ma skyes dgra ni thub pa yis

ya mtshan gyur zhing de nas dga' ba skyes pa ste
sangs rgyas la ni mchog tu dad pa byas pa'o BCt_21.63

nyon mongs rtsod ldan dus ni nges par log pa na
rdzogs ldan dus ni 'ongs nas slar yang chos don bzhin
de ltar rdzu 'phrul dang ldan snyan grags mchog rnams kyis
rab tu gnas pa'i dka' ldan thub pa mchog 'phel to BCt_21.64

mi dge ba dang yongs su ldan pa'i lha sbyin no
nyon mongs sdig pa'i las ni mang po byas nas ni
mi skyong ste na rgu ba gnyis skyes drang srong gi
dmod pa las bzhin sa yi 'og tu bying bar gyur BCt_21.65

| sangs rgyas kyi spyod pa zhes bya ba'i snyan dngags chen po las | las kyi rgyun gyi le'u ste nyi shu rtsa gcig pa'o ||

de nas 'jig rten rjes bzung nas
dus kyi smra ba rnams kyi mchog
chos kyis sa ni khyab mdzad nas
mya ngan 'da' ba dang mtshungs dgongs BCt_22.1

de nas dus su rgyal khab na
pa tā li yi grong du gshegs
mchod rten pa tā li mtshon pa
der ni 'phags pa de bzhugs so BCt_22.2

dus ni de tshe grong khyer gyi
li tstsha bī ni zhi ba'i phyir
ma ga dhā yi rgyal po yi
blon po char dbyibs kyis byas so BCt_22.3

lha rnams kyis der rang gi nor
nye bar len pa rab gzigs nas
grong de 'gron phul byung du
de bzhin gshegs pas rnam par gsungs BCt_22.4

de tshe char pa'i rnam pa yis
bkur byas byed pa rnams kyi mchog
rgya mtsho'i chung ma gtso bo la
mngon phyogs slob ma dang bcas gshegs BCt_22.5

ga-nggā'i 'gram du de gshegs nas
ji ltar rnyed gru de dang des
skye bo rnams ni sgrol ba gzigs
de rnams gzigs nas thugs mdzad do BCt_22.7

'bad pas chu bo sgrol ba la
bdag gi de ltar 'dra ba yin
de phyir rdzu 'phrul mthu yis ni
bdag gi gru med rab tu 'gro BCt_22.8

de ltar der ni slob mar bcas
lha mi rnams la mi snang zhing
rlung gis 'gros kyang phan mdzad nas
skad cig gis ni pha rol gyur BCt_22.9

sdug bsngal mtsho yi pha rol sngon
ye shes gru bos de mkhyen nas
slar yang gru 'di ma dmigs nas
thub pas ga-nggā bsgral ba'o BCt_22.10

bcom ldan nyi ma mdzes pa ni
gang gi sgo las nges 'byung ba
de ni tshe gau ta ma sgor
de la mchod don nyid du byas BCt_22.6

'gram gang dag las rnam 'dren pa
ga-nggā'i pha rol tu gshegs pa
de ni stegs su 'gro la grags
de yi rigs kyis mngon par brjod BCt_22.11

de nas sgrol 'dod mi rnams dang
rgal ba rnams dang sgrol ba rnams
ya mtshan rnam rgyas gdong rnams kyi
mig rnams de la btung bar gyur BCt_22.12

de nas ga-nggā'i 'gram nas ni
sangs rgyas ku ḍa'i grong du gshegs
der ni chos ldan gtam mdzad nas
nā dā'i kar ni mngon par gshegs BCt_22.13

dus ni de tshe de na ni
skye bo chen po rgud pa ste
gang gis gang du gang 'gro
de rnams la der thubs gsungs BCt_22.14

yangs pa can gyi grong du gshegs
de nas a mra skyong ba'i sa
dpal ldan tshal du dpal stug gshegs BCt_22.15

a mra skyong ma res ma'i gtso
rnam par 'dren pa der thos nas
rnam dul theg pa la gnas nas
mchog tu dga' bas rab tu song BCt_22.16

lha yi bya ba'i dus su ni
legs ma rigs kyi mna' ma 'dra BCt_22.17

rang gi gzugs kyis khengs pa yi
dam pa li tstsha bī rnams kyi
sems rnams dang ni nor rnams dang
yon tan mtha' dag rnams kyis phrogs BCt_22.18

dpal dang mdzes pa brtan pa yis
nags kyi lha mo'i gzugs 'dra ba
de ni theg pa la babs nas
skyen par nags der rab tu zhugs BCt_22.19

rigs kyi mo btsun gdung ba mo
mig rab g.yo ba de gzigs nas
bde bar gshegs pas rnga dbyangs kyis
dge slong rnams la bka' stsal pa BCt_22.20

stobs chung rnams kyi yid kyi rim
a mra skyong ma 'di mngon 'ongs
dran ldan bdud rtsi'i sems ldan rnams c 86b
ye shes kyis ni khyed rnams gnas BCt_22.21

nye sar sbrul ni mchog yin zhing
ral gyi gdengs pa'i dgra mo mchog
dran dang ye shes rnams bral ba'i
nye sar bud med rnams ma yin BCt_22.22

bsdad pa 'am ni nyal ba'am
'gro 'am yang na gnas pa 'am
bud med ri mor bris pas kyang
mi rnams kyi ni yid 'phrog go BCt_22.23

'di rnams zhen pas nyam thag gam
gyen du lag bteg du na yang
skra bkram rnams kyis bsreg pa ru
nus na mo btsun rnams sngon nyid BCt_22.24

pha rol po 'brel rnam mang po'i

de yi rang bzhin ma mthong ste
bud med rnams la byis rnams rmongs BCt_22.25

mi rtag sdug bsngal bdag med dang
mi dge ba zhes mthong nas ni
lha zhing sgom pa po rnams kyi
sems ni zil gyis non ma yin BCt_22.26

gnas de rnams su legs goms blo
spyod yul rnams su ba lang bzhin
lha yi yul rnams kyis 'joms par
nus min mi rnams kyis ci smros BCt_22.27

de phyir shes rab mda' 'dzin zhing
brtson 'grus gzhu ni lag pa na
dran pa'i go cha yongs bgos shing
yul gyi 'du shes can du mnos BCt_22.28

lcags kyi thur ma tsha mo yis
mig la reg pa mchog yin zhing
g.yo ba'i mig can bud med la
ma rungs dran pas lta phyir min BCt_22.29

gal te dus ni de yi tshe
chags pa'i sems kyis dus byed na
dud 'gro 'am ni 'og nyid du
dbang med bcings nas khrid par byed BCt_22.30

de phyir 'jigs pa 'di shes nas
mtshan mar spros pa mi bya zhing
lus po la ni gzugs tsam du
gang gis mthong ba de mthong ngo BCt_22.31

dbang pos 'jig rten na yul rnams
'chi min dbang po rnams des min
gang zhig de rnams la chags gyur
de ni de rnams las 'ching ngo BCt_22.32

ba lang gnyis kyi sbyor ba'i phyir

yul dang dbang po de dag ni
chags pa phan tshun de ltar min BCt_22.33

mig gis gzugs ni 'dzin pa ste
sems kyis rnam par rtog par byed
rnam par rtog las der skye zhing
chags dang chags bral nyid kyang ngo BCt_22.34

rnam par ma brtags dbang po'i don
gal te don med ched gyur na
dbang po'i spyod yul la spyod pa
thams cad don med kyis sbyor to BCt_22.35

de phyir ma dor dran pas dang
bag yod mchog tu 'gro bas dang
rang don rjes su mthong bas dang
gdung med sems kyis bsgom par bya BCt_22.36

de ltar don mthar ma gyur ba'i
dge slong rnams la de rjes bstan
ltos byas a mra skyong ma ni
thal mo sbyar byas nye bar 'ongs BCt_22.37

des ni thugs ni drang srong ma
shing drung gnas pa mthong nas ni
nags kyi yongs su longs spyod kyis
mchog tu rjes su 'dzin pa snyam BCt_22.38

de nas bkur sti mang po las
g.yo yang lta byed rab bkod nas
me tog tsam pa ka rgyas ltar
mgo bos thub pa la phyag tshal BCt_22.39

kun mkhyen gyis kyang rjes gnang ma
de nas sa la bsdad pa ste
de yis blo la bzod gsung gis
thub pas de la bka' stsal to BCt_22.40

bsam pa 'di ni yon tan ldan
rnam dag sems dpa' nyid bstan to
bud med byis pa phul gnas pa
chos la 'dod pa rnyed par dka' BCt_22.41

gal te chos kyi bdag nyid gyur
zhen pas bcom pa'i sems ldan pa'i
na rab mi mo rnams kyis dang
blo ldan mi rnams kyis mtshar cing BCt_22.42

rang bzhin gyis ni blo chung zhing
g.yo ba'i sems ldan lang tsho ma
yul gcig ro yis 'jig rten na
chos shes shes pa ya mtshan no BCt_22.43

khyod kyi chos la yid gyur pa
de ni khyod kyis bdag nyid don
mi rtag gson pa'i 'jig rten na
chos las gzhan na nor yod min BCt_22.44

nad kyis nad med 'joms pa ste
rga bas lang tsho gcod pa nyid
'chi bas srog ni len pa ste
chos kyis rgud pa yod ma yin BCt_22.45

gang phyir dga' ba rnams dang bral
mi dga' ba rnams dang sbyor zhing
mngon par 'dod pa thob pa na
de phyir chos ni mchog tu 'gro BCt_22.46

gzhan dbang sdug bsngal chen po ste
rang dbang mchog tu bde ba nyid
ma nu'i rigs su skyes na yang
bud med thams cad gzhan dbang ngo BCt_22.47

gang phyir gzhan dbang nyid phyir dang
de bzhin phru gu 'dzin pa'i phyir
bud med rnams kyi sdug bsngal lhag 92b
de phyir yang dag nges par 'os BCt_22.48

de ltar thub pa chen po'i gsung
rang bzhin gyis dang mkhas las dang
brtan las byis kyang byis min bzhin
thos shing mngon par dga' ba'o BCt_22.49

de bzhin gshegs pa'i chos kyi smra ba yis

bud med nyid ni smad cing yul las log pa ste
gang gi skye bo'i rten la btsog par byas pa'o BCt_22.50

de nas me tog khur las tsu ta'i mchod sdong bzhin

thub pa chen po la ni gus pas mig zhugs shing
yang yang chos ni rnam par dag pa'i lta bas gnas BCt_22.51

rang bzhin gyis ni ngo tsha dang ldan bud med de

'dam skyes mdzod dang 'dra bas thal mo sbyar nas ni
dal bus smra ba'i skad kyi gdangs kyis gsol ba'o BCt_22.52

bcom ldan don mdzad bdag la rjes su gsung don du

sdug bsngal nye bar zhi ba'i mdzad po 'jig rten na
'bras bur gyur pa'i bdag la 'bras bur mdzad du gsol BCt_22.53

de nas de yi gus pa de ltar gzigs nas dang
sems can rnams ni bza' ba'i dbang nyid mkhyen nas ni g 113b
gsung ma phye nas bde bar gshegs pas de ltar zhes
de la nges par rnam 'gyur brda yis mdzad pa'o BCt_22.54

skad cig mdzad pa dang ldan spyan yangs mchog gi chos mda' zhing
chos kyi snod la des ni dga' zhing mgu la rungs pa ste
gus pas rnyed pa mchog ni rnam par nges shing bstod par gyur BCt_22.55

sangs rgyas kyi spyod pa zhes bya ba'i snyan dngags chen po las | a mra skyong ma'i nags gzigs pa'i le'u ste nyi shu rtsa gnyis pa'o || ||

de nas thub pa'i thugs rig nas
phyag 'tshal nas kyang grong du song
de ni li-tstsha bīs thos nas
lta 'dod sangs rgyas la song ngo BCt_23.1

dkar po'i rta dang shing rta gdugs
phreng ba rgyan dang bgo ba rnams
kha cig kha cig de rnams dang
dmar ser rnams dang de bzhin gzhan BCt_23.2

kha cig bai ḍū-rya ljang dang
gzhan rnams rma bya'i mjug ma ste
de ltar cha lugs rgya chen po
bdag gis dga' byed rnams dang song BCt_23.3

ri mo rnam rgyas ro stod can
gser gyi gnya' shing lag pa rnams
dpal ldan bod ring dngos su ni
de rnams mtho ris bzhin du rdzes BCt_23.4

mtshams sprin rkang la sna tshogs rnams
glog ni rab tu snang ba bzhin
shing rta rnams las babs 'dod pas
de rnams gnas pa rnam par mdzes BCt_23.5

dbu rgyan rnam g.yo rnam btud pa'i
brtan rnams thub la phyag 'tshal nas
nga rgyal ldan rnams rgyags med bzhin
chos la dga' bas de rnams gnas BCt_23.6

nyi ma sprin dang bral ba yi
logs su khyer 'jigs gzhu bzhin du
thub pa'i drung der de rnams kyi
chags bral dkyil 'khor mdzes pa'o BCt_23.7

sa la seng ge gnas pa rnams
gser gyis spras pa'i seng ge'i gdan
seng ge la sogs de rnams la
mi yi seng ges de nas gsungs BCt_23.8

gzugs dang dpal dang stogs la sogs
bkur mang rnams dang ldan pa'i
khyed kyi chos gus 'di gang
de las lhag par mdzes pa nyid BCt_23.9

tshul khrims la sogs yon tan gyis
ji ltar 'jig rten mdzes de ltar
lus ni sna tshogs gos sam rgyan
phreng ba rnams kyis ma yin no BCt_23.10

gang du khyed cag bdag po rnams
chos shes 'dul ba 'dod pa rnams
spong byed pa rnams rjes bzung zhing
skal ba bcas rnams bdag gi lugs BCt_23.11

'phags skyes rnyed par dka' dus su
chos la gnas rnams srung byed gyur
phyis 'byung ma yin yul rnams kyi
skal bas dman pa rnams kyis min BCt_23.12

dpal ldan skal ba chen po rnams
chos shes srung bar byed rnams kyis
bsrung ba nyid kyis yul 'di ni
chos kyis kyang ni rjes su 'dzin BCt_23.13

rlung rnams rgal 'dod pa la rnams
khyu mchog rgal ba rnams kyi bzhin
rgyal po rnams kyis gang bzung ba'i
yul la de nas skye dgu 'gro BCt_23.14

khyed cag rnams la tshul khrims de
rtag par 'gyur bar 'os pa ste
bdag gi don ni 'dod rnams kyi
'dir dang song nas dbrog bya min BCt_23.15

yid ni tshim zhing bkur mang dang
rnyed dang grags dang yid ches nyid
dga' ba nyid dang song nas bde
tshul khrims kyi ni 'bras bu che BCt_23.16

'byung po rgyu dang mi rgyu yi
rten ni ji ltar sa yin pa
de ltar yon tan thams cad kyi
rten ni tshul khrims dam pa'o BCt_23.17

'phur 'dod gshogs pa med pa dang
rgal 'dod gru med ji lta bar
mi ni tshul khrims rnams spangs par
dge legs 'dod pa de ltar shes BCt_23.18

me tog 'bras bus khyab pa'i shing
tsher ma can gyur ji lta bar
thos dang gzugs don phun tshogs pa
tshul khrims 'chal pa de ltar ro BCt_23.19

sna tshogs gos dang rgyan ldan zhing
khang bzangs rnams su gnas na yang
tshul khrims dang ldan skye bo gang
de yi drang srong dang mnyam 'gros BCt_23.20

ngur smrig shing shun zur phud dang
gtsug phud spyi bo ral pa rnams
tshul khrims nyams pa kun rnams kyi
bcos ma nyid du shes par bya BCt_23.21

stegs las dus gsum khrus byas nas
me la lan gnyis bsregs nas dang
gdung ba drag por gdungs nas kyang
tshul khrims med na bdag ma yin BCt_23.22

sha za rnams la lus byin nas
ri yi legs nas bor nas sam
me 'am chur ni bdag mchongs na
tshul khrims med na bdag ma yin BCt_23.23

'bras bu rtsa ba chu za zhing
ri dags bzhin du rtswa za'am
rlung gi bza 'ba 'dod pa yang
tshul khrims med na bdag mi 'gyur BCt_23.24

mi gang tshul khrims kyis dman pa
de ni bya dang ri dwags mtshungs
rdol ba'i snod ni chu yis bzhin
de ni chos kyi snod ma yin BCt_23.25

'jigs pa dang ni gtam ngan dang
yid mi ches dang mi dga' nyid
mngon sum 'dir ni thob pa ste
song nas don med za bar 'gyur BCt_23.26

de phyir tshul khrims gzhom mi bya
'brog dgon dag na lam mkhan bzhin
rang dbang dag ni rnyed dka' ba'i
tshul khrims mtho ris dag na gru BCt_23.27

skyon rnams kyis bcom sems kyis ni
thams cad bcom nas 'jug pa ste
tshul khrims rab tu gnas byas nas
nyon mongs 'joms la 'bad pa gyis BCt_23.28

de phyir dang por nga snyam pa
brgyan par 'dod pas spang bar bya
bsreg bya za ba'i du ba bzhin
yon tan rnams kyis nga snyam nyid BCt_23.29

skar ma nyi ma zla ba rnams
sprin gyi dra ba chen pos bzhin
nga rgyal gyis bcom yon tan rnams
yod par gyur kyang mdzes ma yin BCt_23.30

dregs pa ngo tsha 'joms pa ste
mya ngan gyis gtan dga' bas lus
yon tan rnams kyi rtsa ba nas
'joms phyir nga'o snyam ba skye BCt_23.31

'gran pa dang ldan nga rgyal las
lha min lha rnams kyis bcom zhing
mi skyong pa ta la'i byin pa dang
dong gsum pa rnams zad par gyur BCt_23.32

gang zhig mi rtag dngos rnams su
mchog ni nga yin snyam pa dangd 81b
mi dman pa ni nga zhes snyam
de ni mkhas pa min par rtogs BCt_23.33

gzugs ni brtan pa ma yin zhing
'jig pa'i chos can g.yo ba yis
nga zhes gang zhig nga rgyal te
yongs su rtog pa min gzhan ci BCt_23.34

'dod pa'i 'dod chags stobs ldan pa
rab gab lhan skyes dgra bo ste
bshes min nang na spyod pa bzhin
gang zhig bshes kyi sgo nas 'joms BCt_23.35

'dod chags me dang me nyid ni
sreg pa'i bdag nyid kyis mnyam ste
'dod chags me ni 'bar ba na
mtshan mo de nyid ring bar 'gyur BCt_23.36

'dod chags me'i stobs ji 'dra ba
me yi stobs ni de 'drar smin
me ni chu rnams kyis shes te
'dod chags me ni mtshos kyang min BCt_23.37

dus su nags su mes tshig rnams
nags kyi shing rnams skye ba ste
'dod chags mes tshig blo med rnams
chos la skye ba ma yin no BCt_23.38

chags las bde ba tshol ba ste
bde phyir mi dge ba byed cing
mi dge ba las nga myal bar 'gro
chags pa dang mnyam dgra bo med BCt_23.39

chags las sred pa skye ba ste
sred las 'dod pa rnams la chags
'dod pa rnams las sdug bsngal 'thob
chags pa dang mnyam yul med do BCt_23.40

chags pa zhes bya'i nad chen po
de ni byis pas rtogs ma yin
[.. .. .. .. .. .. .. ]
[.. .. .. .. .. .. .. ] BCt_23.41

mi rtags nyid las mi gtsang las
sdug bsngal nyid las bdag med las
gal te mthong na mi chags te
log pa'i blo yis chags pa'o BCt_23.42

de phyir dngos po la chags pa
gang du nye bar skye ba na
der ni ji ltar 'gyur brtag ste
gyur pa mthong ba zhes brjod do BCt_23.43

yon tan yongs su rtogs pa na
ji ltar chags par nye bar 'gro
yon tan med na yongs rtogs na
de bzhin khro ba 'gugs par byed BCt_23.44

de phyir khro ba spong 'dod pas
zhe sdang yongs su brtag mi bya
dkar min 'gros las dub bzhin
khro ba las ni zhe sdang 'dzag BCt_23.45

khro ba gzugs ldan rnams kyi dga'
mig ldan rnams kyi mun pa yang
chos don 'dod pa rnams kyi gshed
mos pa'i mi mthun pa nyid do BCt_23.46

khro ba blo yi mun pa mchog
mdza' bshes gyur pa'i dgra bo mchog
bkur sti mang po'i gcod pa pod 82a
zil gyis non pa'i byed pa po BCt_23.47

de bzhin khro ba mi bya zhing
byas nas kyang ni dor bar bya
dmug pa'i rang bzhin lto 'phye bzhin
khro ba'i rjes su 'jug mi bya BCt_23.48

skor ba'i shing rta bzhin gang gis
khro ba brtan pas thag pas bzung
de bdag kha lo sgyur snyam ste
cig shos skye bo thag pa 'dzin BCt_23.49

gang zhig khro ba 'dod pa ste
skye ba 'gog pa 'dod ma yin
phyis de khro ba med pa na
me la reg pa bzhin du bsreg BCt_23.50

khro ba skyes pas sngon rol du
bdag nyid kyis ni sems bsreg ste
rnam par 'phel zhing phyin pa ni
gzan ni sreg gam mi sreg gam BCt_23.51

nad sogs nye bar 'tshe rnams kyi
gang tshe 'jig rten brtse ba rnams
lus can bshes ma yin rnams la
gnod sems byas nas yon tan ci BCt_23.52

de phyir 'jig rten sdug bsngal ba
shes nas khro ba zlog pa'i phyir
'byung po kun la byams pa dang
snying rje nyid ni bsgom par bya BCt_23.53

de ltar nyon mongs lhag pa gang
de yi de tshe gzigs pa ste
de la brtse bas sangs rgyas kyis
de rnams la gsungs snad pa'o BCt_23.54

sems can nyam thag rnams la ni
ji ltar rang bzhin gyis mkhas pa'i
sman pas sman ni gsungs pa ste
nad rnams nye bar zhi phyir ro BCt_23.55

de bzhin chags dang rga sogs kyi
nad kyis 'byung po nyam thag la
thub pas bsam pa mkhyen nas ni
de nyid shes pa'i sman byin to BCt_23.56

de ltar thub pa'i gsung la ni
li tstsha bī rnams mngon dga' ste
rab 'phyang gtsug gi nor bu can
mgo bo rnams kyis phyag tshal lo BCt_23.57

de nas thal mo rnam sbyar nas
cung zhig dud pa'i lus rnams kyis
phur bu la ni lha rnams bzhin
sangs rgyas la ni byon par zhus BCt_23.58

dang po a mra skyong ma'i rigs
thub pas de rnams la gsungs shing
dam pa rnams kyis thog mar ni
snyan mnan 'dor bya min par gsungs BCt_23.59

de rnams bud med de yis ni
bdag la bsrungs par shes pa ste
de bzhin gshegs la mchod mang po
nyis 'gyur nyid du byas pa'o BCt_23.60

legs brjod drang srong sngags rnams kyis
sbrul rnams kyi ni dug bzhin du
kun mkhyen gyis bstan de rnams ni
rab tu zhi ba'i yid rnams song BCt_23.61

de yi mtshan mo 'das nas ni
a mra skyong mas bkur byas te
'od ma ldan pa'i grong du ni
[.. .. .. .. .. .. .. ] BCt_23.62

dbyar rnams rnam par 'das pa na
yangs pa can nyid du gshegs shing
spre'u rdzing gi 'gram du ni
thub pa chen po bzhugs pa'o BCt_23.63

shing gi rtsa bar de bzhugs so
de bzhin du ni 'bar ba la
nags tshal de ni snang byas shing
nye bar 'ongs nas bdud kyis smras BCt_23.64

nai ra-nydza na'i 'gram du sngon
thub pa khyod la bdag gis smras
bya ba byas pa mya ngan zlos
zhes 'dir khyod kyis lan smras so BCt_23.65

nyam thag pa rnams 'jigs med cing
nyan thos rnams ni don byas par
bdag gis ji srid ma gyur pa
de srid mya ngan mi 'da' zhes BCt_23.66

de 'di mang po rnams grol zhing
de bzhin grol bar 'dod rnams dang
grol bar gyur pa rnams nyid de
de phyir mya ngan 'da' bar 'os BCt_23.67

de nas tshig 'di gsan gyur nas
zla ba gsum na mya ngan 'da'
mi brtan pa ni dor cig ces
dgra bcom rnams kyi mchog gis gsungs BCt_23.68

de nas dam bca' 'di shes nas
yid la re ba gang ba ste
rab tu dga' zhing mgu ba ni
de nyid du ni mi snang gyur BCt_23.69

de nas drang srong chen po'i thugs kyi ting nge 'dzin
rnam pa de ltar rnal 'byor stobs las mdzad pa nyid
sku tshe ji ltar gyur pa sngon du btang ba ste
rdzu 'phrul mthu las mtshungs pa med pa 'tsho bar gyur BCt_23.70

des ni sku tshe btang ba'i yud tsam de la ni
bud med myos ma bzhin du sa ni g.yos gyur la
ma yis tshos pa'i lhun po'i rdo ba rim bzhin du
phyogs rnams dag las sgron ma chen po rnams lhung ngo BCt_23.71

de bzhin kun nas dbang po'i rdo rje mi bzad rnams
glog dang bcas shing mi yi snying po can g.yos shing
bskal pa 'jig che 'jig rten bsreg par 'dod pa bzhin
phyogs rnams thams cad rnams su me dag 'bar bar gyur BCt_23.72

shing rnams kyis ni phung po 'gogs pa rnams por zhing
ri rnams kyis ni rtsi mo rnams ni dor ba ste
rlung gis mngon par gang ba'i rdo ba'i phug bzhin du
mkha' la rnga rnams kyi ni ma rungs sgra rnams bsgrags BCt_23.73

de nas de ltar kun tu bskyod tshe yud tsam la
mi yi 'jig rten na dang lha dang nam mkha' la
ting nge 'dzin chen po las rnam par bzhengs mdzad nas
thub pa chen pos gsung ni 'di nyid gsungs pa'o BCt_23.74

shing rta srog shing rnam par jams pa dang 'dra ba'i
tshe btang lus po nang gi stobs las 'dren bgyi zhing
sgo nga'i skye gnas pa rnams sgo nga phye nas bzhin
srid pa'i 'ching las tshe dang lhan cig 'grol bar bgyi BCt_23.75

sangs rgyas kyi spyod pa zhes bya ba'i snyan dngags chen po las | sku tshe'i 'du byed byin gyis brlabs pa'i le'u ste nyi shu rtsa gsum pa'o || ||
